1     !      SUBROUTINE JCG (NN,IA,JA,A,RHS,U,IWKSP,NW,WKSP,IPARM,RPARM,IERR)
2     !C       
3     !C     ITPACK 2C MAIN SUBROUTINE  JCG  (JACOBI CONJUGATE GRADIENT)   
4     !C     EACH OF THE MAIN SUBROUTINES:   
5     !C           JCG, JSI, SOR, SSORCG, SSORSI, RSCG, RSSI     
6     !C     CAN BE USED INDEPENDENTLY OF THE OTHERS   
7     !C       
8     !C ... FUNCTION:   
9     !C       
10     !C          THIS SUBROUTINE, JCG, DRIVES THE JACOBI CONJUGATE
11     !C          GRADIENT ALGORITHM.
12     !C       
13     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
14     !C       
15     !C          N      INPUT INTEGER.  DIMENSION OF THE MATRIX. (= NN)   
16     !C          IA,JA  INPUT INTEGER VECTORS.  THE TWO INTEGER ARRAYS OF 
17     !C                 THE SPARSE MATRIX REPRESENTATION.       
18     !C          A      INPUT D.P. VECTOR.  THE D.P. ARRAY OF THE SPARSE  
19     !C                 MATRIX REPRESENTATION.
20     !C          RHS    INPUT D.P. VECTOR.  CONTAINS THE RIGHT HAND SIDE  
21     !C                 OF THE MATRIX PROBLEM.
22     !C          U      INPUT/OUTPUT D.P. VECTOR.  ON INPUT, U CONTAINS THE 
23     !C                 INITIAL GUESS TO THE SOLUTION. ON OUTPUT, IT CONTAINS 
24     !C                 THE LATEST ESTIMATE TO THE SOLUTION.    
25     !C          IWKSP  INTEGER VECTOR WORKSPACE OF LENGTH 3*N  
26     !C          NW     INPUT INTEGER.  LENGTH OF AVAILABLE WKSP.  ON OUTPUT, 
27     !C                 IPARM(8) IS AMOUNT USED.      
28     !C          WKSP   D.P. VECTOR USED FOR WORKING SPACE.  JACOBI CONJUGATE 
29     !C                 GRADIENT NEEDS THIS TO BE IN LENGTH AT LEAST      
30     !C                 4*N + 2*ITMAX,  IF ISYM = 0  (SYMMETRIC STORAGE)  
31     !C                 4*N + 4*ITMAX,  IF ISYM = 1  (NONSYMMETRIC STORAGE) 
32     !C                 HERE ITMAX = IPARM(1) AND ISYM = IPARM(5) 
33     !C                 (ITMAX IS THE MAXIMUM ALLOWABLE NUMBER OF ITERATIONS) 
34     !C          IPARM  INTEGER VECTOR OF LENGTH 12.  ALLOWS USER TO SPECIFY
35     !C                 SOME INTEGER PARAMETERS WHICH AFFECT THE METHOD.  
36     !C          RPARM  D.P. VECTOR OF LENGTH 12. ALLOWS USER TO SPECIFY SOME 
37     !C                 D.P. PARAMETERS WHICH AFFECT THE METHOD.
38     !C          IER    OUTPUT INTEGER.  ERROR FLAG. (= IERR)   
39     !C       
40     !C ... JCG SUBPROGRAM REFERENCES:      
41     !C       
42     !C          FROM ITPACK    BISRCH, CHGCON, DETERM, DFAULT, ECHALL,   
43     !C                         ECHOUT, EIGVNS, EIGVSS, EQRT1S, ITERM, TIMER, 
44     !C                         ITJCG, IVFILL, PARCON, PERMAT,  
45     !C                         PERROR, PERVEC, PJAC, PMULT, PRBNDX,      
46     !C                         PSTOP, QSORT, DAXPY, SBELM, SCAL, DCOPY,  
47     !C                         DDOT, SUM3, UNSCAL, VEVMW, VFILL, VOUT,   
48     !C                         WEVMW, ZBRENT 
49     !C          SYSTEM         DABS, DLOG10, DBLE(AMAX0), DMAX1, MOD, DSQRT
50     !C       
51     !C     VERSION:  ITPACK 2C (MARCH 1982)
52     !C       
53     !C     CODE WRITTEN BY:  DAVID KINCAID, ROGER GRIMES, JOHN RESPESS   
54     !C                       CENTER FOR NUMERICAL ANALYSIS     
55     !C                       UNIVERSITY OF TEXAS     
56     !C                       AUSTIN, TX  78712       
57     !C                       (512) 471-1242
58     !C       
59     !C     FOR ADDITIONAL DETAILS ON THE   
60     !C          (A) SUBROUTINE SEE TOMS ARTICLE 1982 
61     !C          (B) ALGORITHM  SEE CNA REPORT 150    
62     !C       
63     !C     BASED ON THEORY BY:  DAVID YOUNG, DAVID KINCAID, LOU HAGEMAN  
64     !C       
65     !C     REFERENCE THE BOOK:  APPLIED ITERATIVE METHODS      
66     !C                          L. HAGEMAN, D. YOUNG 
67     !C                          ACADEMIC PRESS, 1981 
68     !C       
69     !C     **************************************************  
70     !C     *               IMPORTANT NOTE                   *  
71     !C     *                                                *  
72     !C     *      WHEN INSTALLING ITPACK ROUTINES ON A      *  
73     !C     *  DIFFERENT COMPUTER, RESET SOME OF THE VALUES  *  
74     !C     *  IN  SUBROUTNE DFAULT.   MOST IMPORTANT ARE    *  
75     !C     *                                                *  
76     !C     *   DRELPR      MACHINE RELATIVE PRECISION       *  
77     !C     *   RPARM(1)    STOPPING CRITERION               *  
78     !C     *                                                *  
79     !C     *   ALSO CHANGE SYSTEM-DEPENDENT ROUTINE         *  
80     !C     *   SECOND USED IN TIMER                         *  
81     !C     *                                                *  
82     !C     **************************************************  
83     !C       
84     !C     SPECIFICATIONS FOR ARGUMENTS    
85     !C       
86     !      INTEGER IA(1),JA(1),IWKSP(1),IPARM(12),NN,NW,IERR   
87     !      DOUBLE PRECISION A(1),RHS(NN),U(NN),WKSP(NW),RPARM(12)
88     !C       
89     !C     SPECIFICATIONS FOR LOCAL VARIABLES
90     !C       
91     !      INTEGER IB1,IB2,IB3,IB4,IB5,IDGTS,IER,IERPER,ITMAX1,LOOP,N,NB,N3
92     !      DOUBLE PRECISION DIGIT1,DIGIT2,TEMP,TIME1,TIME2,TOL 
93     !C       
94     !C **** BEGIN: ITPACK COMMON 
95     !C       
96     !      INTEGER IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT       
97     !      COMMON /ITCOM1/ IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT 
98     !C       
99     !      LOGICAL ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD   
100     !      COMMON /ITCOM2/ ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD     
101     !C       
102     !      DOUBLE PRECISION BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA,
103     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
104     !      COMMON /ITCOM3/ BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA, 
105     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
106     !C       
107     !C **** END  : ITPACK COMMON 
108     !C       
109     !C ... VARIABLES IN COMMON BLOCK - ITCOM1
110     !C       
111     !C     IN     - ITERATION NUMBER       
112     !C     IS     - ITERATION NUMBER WHEN PARAMETERS LAST CHANGED
113     !C     ISYM   - SYMMETRIC/NONSYMMETRIC STORAGE FORMAT SWITCH 
114     !C     ITMAX  - MAXIMUM NUMBER OF ITERATIONS ALLOWED       
115     !C     LEVEL  - LEVEL OF OUTPUT CONTROL SWITCH   
116     !C     NOUT   - OUTPUT UNIT NUMBER     
117     !C       
118     !C ... VARIABLES IN COMMON BLOCK - ITCOM2
119     !C       
120     !C     ADAPT  - FULLY ADAPTIVE PROCEDURE SWITCH  
121     !C     BETADT - SWITCH FOR ADAPTIVE DETERMINATION OF BETA  
122     !C     CASEII - ADAPTIVE PROCEDURE CASE SWITCH   
123     !C     HALT   - STOPPING TEST SWITCH   
124     !C     PARTAD - PARTIALLY ADAPTIVE PROCEDURE SWITCH
125     !C       
126     !C ... VARIABLES IN COMMON BLOCK - ITCOM3
127     !C       
128     !C     BDELNM - TWO NORM OF B TIMES DELTA-SUPER-N
129     !C     BETAB  - ESTIMATE FOR THE SPECTRAL RADIUS OF LU MATRIX
130     !C     CME    - ESTIMATE OF LARGEST EIGENVALUE   
131     !C     DELNNM - INNER PRODUCT OF PSEUDO-RESIDUAL AT ITERATION N      
132     !C     DELSNM - INNER PRODUCT OF PSEUDO-RESIDUAL AT ITERATION S

143     !C     DRELPR - MACHINE RELATIVE PRECISION       
144     !C     STPTST - STOPPING PARAMETER     
145     !C     UDNM   - TWO NORM OF U
146     !C     ZETA   - STOPPING CRITERION

167     !     *   ' (ZETA)'/' ','    A VALUE THIS SMALL MAY HINDER CONVERGENCE '/

390     !      SUBROUTINE JSI (NN,IA,JA,A,RHS,U,IWKSP,NW,WKSP,IPARM,RPARM,IERR)
391     !C       
392     !C     ITPACK 2C MAIN SUBROUTINE  JSI  (JACOBI SEMI-ITERATIVE)       
393     !C     EACH OF THE MAIN SUBROUTINES:   
394     !C           JCG, JSI, SOR, SSORCG, SSORSI, RSCG, RSSI     
395     !C     CAN BE USED INDEPENDENTLY OF THE OTHERS   
396     !C       
397     !C ... FUNCTION:   
398     !C       
399     !C          THIS SUBROUTINE, JSI, DRIVES THE JACOBI SEMI-  
400     !C          ITERATION ALGORITHM.       
401     !C       
402     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
403     !C       
404     !C          N      INPUT INTEGER.  DIMENSION OF THE MATRIX. (= NN)   
405     !C          IA,JA  INPUT INTEGER VECTORS.  THE TWO INTEGER ARRAYS OF 
406     !C                 THE SPARSE MATRIX REPRESENTATION.       
407     !C          A      INPUT D.P. VECTOR.  THE D.P. ARRAY OF THE SPARSE  
408     !C                 MATRIX REPRESENTATION.
409     !C          RHS    INPUT D.P. VECTOR.  CONTAINS THE RIGHT HAND SIDE  
410     !C                 OF THE MATRIX PROBLEM.
411     !C          U      INPUT/OUTPUT D.P. VECTOR.  ON INPUT, U CONTAINS THE 
412     !C                 INITIAL GUESS TO THE SOLUTION. ON OUTPUT, IT CONTAINS 
413     !C                 THE LATEST ESTIMATE TO THE SOLUTION.

423     !C                 D.P. PARAMETERS WHICH AFFECT THE METHOD.

759     !      SUBROUTINE SOR (NN,IA,JA,A,RHS,U,IWKSP,NW,WKSP,IPARM,RPARM,IERR)
760     !C       
761     !C     ITPACK 2C MAIN SUBROUTINE  SOR  (SUCCESSIVE OVERRELATION)     
762     !C     EACH OF THE MAIN SUBROUTINES:   
763     !C           JCG, JSI, SOR, SSORCG, SSORSI, RSCG, RSSI     
764     !C     CAN BE USED INDEPENDENTLY OF THE OTHERS   
765     !C       
766     !C ... FUNCTION:   
767     !C       
768     !C          THIS SUBROUTINE, SOR, DRIVES THE  SUCCESSIVE   
769     !C          OVERRELAXATION ALGORITHM.  
770     !C       
771     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
772     !C       
773     !C          N      INPUT INTEGER.  DIMENSION OF THE MATRIX. (= NN)   
774     !C          IA,JA  INPUT INTEGER VECTORS.  THE TWO INTEGER ARRAYS OF 
775     !C                 THE SPARSE MATRIX REPRESENTATION.       
776     !C          A      INPUT D.P. VECTOR.  THE D.P. ARRAY OF THE SPARSE  
777     !C                 MATRIX REPRESENTATION 
778     !C          RHS    INPUT D.P. VECTOR.  CONTAINS THE RIGHT HAND SIDE  
779     !C                 OF THE MATRIX PROBLEM.
780     !C          U      INPUT/OUTPUT D.P. VECTOR.  ON INPUT, U CONTAINS THE 
781     !C                 INITIAL GUESS TO THE SOLUTION. ON OUTPUT, IT CONTAINS 
782     !C                 THE LATEST ESTIMATE TO THE SOLUTION.    
783     !C          IWKSP  INTEGER VECTOR WORKSPACE OF LENGTH 3*N  
784     !C          NW     INPUT INTEGER.  LENGTH OF AVAILABLE WKSP.  ON OUTPUT, 
785     !C                 IPARM(8) IS AMOUNT USED.      
786     !C          WKSP   D.P. VECTOR USED FOR WORKING SPACE.  SOR NEEDS THIS 
787     !C                 TO BE IN LENGTH AT LEAST  N   
788     !C          IPARM  INTEGER VECTOR OF LENGTH 12.  ALLOWS USER TO SPECIFY
789     !C                 SOME INTEGER PARAMETERS WHICH AFFECT THE METHOD.  
790     !C          RPARM  D.P. VECTOR OF LENGTH 12. ALLOWS USER TO SPECIFY SOME 
791     !C                 D.P. PARAMETERS WHICH AFFECT THE METHOD.
792     !C          IER    OUTPUT INTEGER.  ERROR FLAG. (= IERR)   
793     !C       
794     !C ... SOR SUBPROGRAM REFERENCES:      
795     !C       
796     !C          FROM ITPACK   BISRCH, DFAULT, ECHALL, ECHOUT, IPSTR, ITERM,
797     !C                        TIMER, ITSOR, IVFILL, PERMAT, PERROR,      
798     !C                        PERVEC, PFSOR1, PMULT, PRBNDX, PSTOP, QSORT, 
799     !C                        SBELM, SCAL, DCOPY, DDOT, TAU, UNSCAL, VFILL,
800     !C                        VOUT, WEVMW  
801     !C          SYSTEM        DABS, DLOG10, DBLE(AMAX0), DMAX1, DBLE(FLOAT), 
802     !C                        DSQRT
803     !C       
804     !C     VERSION:  ITPACK 2C (MARCH 1982)
805     !C       
806     !C     CODE WRITTEN BY:  DAVID KINCAID, ROGER GRIMES, JOHN RESPESS   
807     !C                       CENTER FOR NUMERICAL ANALYSIS     
808     !C                       UNIVERSITY OF TEXAS     
809     !C                       AUSTIN, TX  78712       
810     !C                       (512) 471-1242
811     !C       
812     !C     FOR ADDITIONAL DETAILS ON THE   
813     !C          (A) SUBROUTINE SEE TOMS ARTICLE 1982 
814     !C          (B) ALGORITHM  SEE CNA REPORT 150    
815     !C       
816     !C     BASED ON THEORY BY:  DAVID YOUNG, DAVID KINCAID, LOU HAGEMAN  
817     !C       
818     !C     REFERENCE THE BOOK:  APPLIED ITERATIVE METHODS      
819     !C                          L. HAGEMAN, D. YOUNG 
820     !C                          ACADEMIC PRESS, 1981 
821     !C       
822     !C     **************************************************  
823     !C     *               IMPORTANT NOTE                   *  
824     !C     *                                                *  
825     !C     *      WHEN INSTALLING ITPACK ROUTINES ON A      *  
826     !C     *  DIFFERENT COMPUTER, RESET SOME OF THE VALUES  *  
827     !C     *  IN  SUBROUTNE DFAULT.   MOST IMPORTANT ARE    *  
828     !C     *                                                *  
829     !C     *   DRELPR      MACHINE RELATIVE PRECISION       *  
830     !C     *   RPARM(1)    STOPPING CRITERION               *  
831     !C     *                                                *

1112     !      SUBROUTINE SSORCG (NN,IA,JA,A,RHS,U,IWKSP,NW,WKSP,IPARM,RPARM,
1113     !     *   IERR)    
1114     !C       
1115     !C     ITPACK 2C MAIN SUBROUTINE  SSORCG  (SYMMETRIC SUCCESSIVE OVER-
1116     !C                                        RELAXATION CONJUGATE GRADIENT) 
1117     !C     EACH OF THE MAIN SUBROUTINES:   
1118     !C           JCG, JSI, SOR, SSORCG, SSORSI, RSCG, RSSI     
1119     !C     CAN BE USED INDEPENDENTLY OF THE OTHERS   
1120     !C       
1121     !C ... FUNCTION:   
1122     !C       
1123     !C          THIS SUBROUTINE, SSORCG, DRIVES THE  SYMMETRIC SOR-CG    
1124     !C          ALGORITHM.       
1125     !C       
1126     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
1127     !C       
1128     !C          N      INPUT INTEGER.  DIMENSION OF THE MATRIX. (= NN)   
1129     !C          IA,JA  INPUT INTEGER VECTORS.  THE TWO INTEGER ARRAYS OF 
1130     !C                 THE SPARSE MATRIX REPRESENTATION.       
1131     !C          A      INPUT D.P. VECTOR.  THE D.P. ARRAY OF THE SPARSE  
1132     !C                 MATRIX REPRESENTATION.
1133     !C          RHS    INPUT D.P. VECTOR.  CONTAINS THE RIGHT HAND SIDE  
1134     !C                 OF THE MATRIX PROBLEM.
1135     !C          U      INPUT/OUTPUT D.P. VECTOR.  ON INPUT, U CONTAINS THE 
1136     !C                 INITIAL GUESS TO THE SOLUTION. ON OUTPUT, IT CONTAINS 
1137     !C                 THE LATEST ESTIMATE TO THE SOLUTION.    
1138     !C          IWKSP  INTEGER VECTOR WORKSPACE OF LENGTH 3*N  
1139     !C          NW     INPUT INTEGER.  LENGTH OF AVAILABLE WKSP.  ON OUTPUT, 
1140     !C                 IPARM(8) IS AMOUNT USED.      
1141     !C          WKSP   D.P. VECTOR USED FOR WORKING SPACE.  SSOR-CG      
1142     !C                 NEEDS TO BE IN LENGTH AT LEAST
1143     !C                 6*N + 2*ITMAX,  IF IPARM(5)=0  (SYMMETRIC STORAGE)
1144     !C                 6*N + 4*ITMAX,  IF IPARM(5)=1  (NONSYMMETRIC STORAGE) 
1145     !C          IPARM  INTEGER VECTOR OF LENGTH 12.  ALLOWS USER TO SPECIFY
1146     !C                 SOME INTEGER PARAMETERS WHICH AFFECT THE METHOD.  IF
1147     !C          RPARM  D.P. VECTOR OF LENGTH 12. ALLOWS USER TO SPECIFY SOME 
1148     !C                 D.P. PARAMETERS WHICH AFFECT THE METHOD.
1149     !C          IER    OUTPUT INTEGER.  ERROR FLAG. (= IERR)   
1150     !C       
1151     !C ... SSORCG SUBPROGRAM REFERENCES:   
1152     !C       
1153     !C          FROM ITPACK    BISRCH, CHGCON, DETERM, DFAULT, ECHALL,   
1154     !C                         ECHOUT, EIGVNS, EIGVSS, EQRT1S, ITERM, TIMER, 
1155     !C                         ITSRCG, IVFILL, OMEG, OMGCHG, OMGSTR,     
1156     !C                         PARCON, PBETA, PBSOR, PERMAT, PERROR,     
1157     !C                         PERVEC, PFSOR, PJAC, PMULT, PRBNDX, PSTOP, PVT
1158     !C                         QSORT, SBELM, SCAL, DCOPY, DDOT, SUM3,    
1159     !C                         UNSCAL, VEVMW, VEVPW, VFILL, VOUT, WEVMW, 
1160     !C                         ZBRENT      
1161     !C          SYSTEM         DABS, DLOG, DLOG10, DBLE(AMAX0), DMAX1, AMIN1,
1162     !C                         MOD, DSQRT  
1163     !C       
1164     !C     VERSION:  ITPACK 2C (MARCH 1982)
1165     !C       
1166     !C     CODE WRITTEN BY:  DAVID KINCAID, ROGER GRIMES, JOHN RESPESS   
1167     !C                       CENTER FOR NUMERICAL ANALYSIS     
1168     !C                       UNIVERSITY OF TEXAS     
1169     !C                       AUSTIN, TX  78712       
1170     !C                       (512) 471-1242
1171     !C       
1172     !C     FOR ADDITIONAL DETAILS ON THE   
1173     !C          (A) SUBROUTINE SEE TOMS ARTICLE 1982 
1174     !C          (B) ALGORITHM  SEE CNA REPORT 150    
1175     !C       
1176     !C     BASED ON THEORY BY:  DAVID YOUNG, DAVID KINCAID, LOU HAGEMAN  
1177     !C       
1178     !C     REFERENCE THE BOOK:  APPLIED ITERATIVE METHODS      
1179     !C                          L. HAGEMAN, D. YOUNG 
1180     !C                          ACADEMIC PRESS, 1981 
1181     !C       
1182     !C     **************************************************  
1183     !C     *               IMPORTANT NOTE                   *  
1184     !C     *                                                *  
1185     !C     *      WHEN INSTALLING ITPACK ROUTINES ON A      *  
1186     !C     *  DIFFERENT COMPUTER, RESET SOME OF THE VALUES  *  
1187     !C     *  IN  SUBROUTNE DFAULT.   MOST IMPORTANT ARE    *  
1188     !C     *                                                *  
1189     !C     *   DRELPR      MACHINE RELATIVE PRECISION       *  
1190     !C     *   RPARM(1)    STOPPING CRITERION               *  
1191     !C     *                                                *  
1192     !C     *   ALSO CHANGE SYSTEM-DEPENDENT ROUTINE         *  
1193     !C     *   SECOND USED IN TIMER                         *  
1194     !C     *                                                *  
1195     !C     **************************************************  
1196     !C       
1197     !C     SPECIFICATIONS FOR ARGUMENTS    
1198     !C       
1199     !      INTEGER IA(1),JA(1),IWKSP(1),IPARM(12),NN,NW,IERR   
1200     !      DOUBLE PRECISION A(1),RHS(NN),U(NN),WKSP(NW),RPARM(12)
1201     !C       
1202     !C     SPECIFICATIONS FOR LOCAL VARIABLES
1203     !C       
1204     !      INTEGER IB1,IB2,IB3,IB4,IB5,IB6,IB7,IDGTS,IER,IERPER,ITMAX1,LOOP,N
1205     !     *   ,NB,N3   
1206     !      DOUBLE PRECISION BETNEW,DIGIT1,DIGIT2,PBETA,TEMP,TIME1,TIME2,TOL
1207     !C       
1208     !C *** BEGIN: ITPACK COMMON  
1209     !C       
1210     !      INTEGER IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT       
1211     !      COMMON /ITCOM1/ IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT 
1212     !C       
1213     !      LOGICAL ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD   
1214     !      COMMON /ITCOM2/ ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD     
1215     !C       
1216     !      DOUBLE PRECISION BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA,
1217     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
1218     !      COMMON /ITCOM3/ BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA, 
1219     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
1220     !C       
1221     !C *** END  : ITPACK COMMON  
1222     !C       
1223     !C ... VARIABLES IN COMMON BLOCK - ITCOM1
1224     !C       
1225     !C     IN     - ITERATION NUMBER       
1226     !C     IS     - ITERATION NUMBER WHEN PARAMETERS LAST CHANGED
1227     !C     ISYM   - SYMMETRIC/NONSYMMETRIC STORAGE FORMAT SWITCH 
1228     !C     ITMAX  - MAXIMUM NUMBER OF ITERATIONS ALLOWED       
1229     !C     LEVEL  - LEVEL OF OUTPUT CONTROL SWITCH

1521     !      SUBROUTINE SSORSI (NN,IA,JA,A,RHS,U,IWKSP,NW,WKSP,IPARM,RPARM,
1522     !     *   IERR)    
1523     !C       
1524     !C     ITPACK 2C MAIN SUBROUTINE  SSORSI  (SYMMETRIC SUCCESSIVE RELAX- 
1525     !C                                         ATION SEMI-ITERATION)     
1526     !C     EACH OF THE MAIN SUBROUTINES:   
1527     !C           JCG, JSI, SOR, SSORCG, SSORSI, RSCG, RSSI     
1528     !C     CAN BE USED INDEPENDENTLY OF THE OTHERS   
1529     !C       
1530     !C ... FUNCTION:   
1531     !C       
1532     !C          THIS SUBROUTINE, SSORSI, DRIVES THE  SYMMETRIC SOR-SI    
1533     !C          ALGORITHM.       
1534     !C       
1535     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
1536     !C       
1537     !C          N      INPUT INTEGER.  DIMENSION OF THE MATRIX. (= NN)   
1538     !C          IA,JA  INPUT INTEGER VECTORS.  THE TWO INTEGER ARRAYS OF 
1539     !C                 THE SPARSE MATRIX REPRESENTATION.       
1540     !C          A      INPUT D.P. VECTOR.  THE D.P. ARRAY OF THE SPARSE  
1541     !C                 MATRIX REPRESENTATION.
1542     !C          RHS    INPUT D.P. VECTOR.  CONTAINS THE RIGHT HAND SIDE  
1543     !C                 OF THE MATRIX PROBLEM.
1544     !C          U      INPUT/OUTPUT D.P. VECTOR.  ON INPUT, U CONTAINS THE 
1545     !C                 INITIAL GUESS TO THE SOLUTION. ON OUTPUT, IT CONTAINS 
1546     !C                 THE LATEST ESTIMATE TO THE SOLUTION.    
1547     !C          IWKSP  INTEGER VECTOR WORKSPACE OF LENGTH 3*N  
1548     !C          NW     INPUT INTEGER.  LENGTH OF AVAILABLE WKSP.  ON OUTPUT, 
1549     !C                 IPARM(8) IS AMOUNT USED.      
1550     !C          WKSP   D.P. VECTOR USED FOR WORKING SPACE.  SSORSI       
1551     !C                 NEEDS THIS TO BE IN LENGTH AT LEAST  5*N
1552     !C          IPARM  INTEGER VECTOR OF LENGTH 12.  ALLOWS USER TO SPECIFY
1553     !C                 SOME INTEGER PARAMETERS WHICH AFFECT THE METHOD.  IF
1554     !C          RPARM  D.P. VECTOR OF LENGTH 12. ALLOWS USER TO SPECIFY SOME 
1555     !C                 D.P. PARAMETERS WHICH AFFECT THE METHOD.
1556     !C          IER    OUTPUT INTEGER.  ERROR FLAG. (= IERR)   
1557     !C       
1558     !C ... SSORSI SUBPROGRAM REFERENCES:   
1559     !C       
1560     !C          FROM ITPACK    BISRCH, CHEBY, CHGSI, DFAULT, ECHALL, ECHOUT, 
1561     !C                         ITERM, TIMER, ITSRSI, IVFILL, OMEG,       
1562     !C                         OMGSTR, PARSI, PBETA, PERMAT, PERROR,     
1563     !C                         PERVEC, PFSOR, PMULT, PRBNDX, PSSOR1,     
1564     !C                         PSTOP, PVTBV, QSORT, SBELM, SCAL, DCOPY,  
1565     !C                         DDOT, SUM3, TSTCHG, UNSCAL, VEVPW, VFILL, 
1566     !C                         VOUT, WEVMW 
1567     !C          SYSTEM         DABS, DLOG, DLOG10, DBLE(AMAX0), DMAX1, DBLE(F
1568     !C                         MOD, DSQRT  
1569     !C       
1570     !C     VERSION:  ITPACK 2C (MARCH 1982)
1571     !C       
1572     !C     CODE WRITTEN BY:  DAVID KINCAID, ROGER GRIMES, JOHN RESPESS   
1573     !C                       CENTER FOR NUMERICAL ANALYSIS     
1574     !C                       UNIVERSITY OF TEXAS     
1575     !C                       AUSTIN, TX  78712       
1576     !C                       (512) 471-1242
1577     !C       
1578     !C     FOR ADDITIONAL DETAILS ON THE   
1579     !C          (A) SUBROUTINE SEE TOMS ARTICLE 1982 
1580     !C          (B) ALGORITHM  SEE CNA REPORT 150    
1581     !C       
1582     !C     BASED ON THEORY BY:  DAVID YOUNG, DAVID KINCAID, LOU HAGEMAN  
1583     !C       
1584     !C     REFERENCE THE BOOK:  APPLIED ITERATIVE METHODS      
1585     !C                          L. HAGEMAN, D. YOUNG 
1586     !C                          ACADEMIC PRESS, 1981 
1587     !C       
1588     !C     **************************************************  
1589     !C     *               IMPORTANT NOTE                   *  
1590     !C     *                                                *  
1591     !C     *      WHEN INSTALLING ITPACK ROUTINES ON A      *  
1592     !C     *  DIFFERENT COMPUTER, RESET SOME OF THE VALUES  *  
1593     !C     *  IN  SUBROUTNE DFAULT.   MOST IMPORTANT ARE    *  
1594     !C     *                                                *  
1595     !C     *   DRELPR      MACHINE RELATIVE PRECISION       *  
1596     !C     *   RPARM(1)    STOPPING CRITERION               *  
1597     !C     *                                                *  
1598     !C     *   ALSO CHANGE SYSTEM-DEPENDENT ROUTINE         *  
1599     !C     *   SECOND USED IN TIMER                         *  
1600     !C     *                                                *  
1601     !C     **************************************************  
1602     !C       
1603     !C     SPECIFICATIONS FOR ARGUMENTS    
1604     !C       
1605     !      INTEGER IA(1),JA(1),IWKSP(1),IPARM(12),NN,NW,IERR   
1606     !      DOUBLE PRECISION A(1),RHS(NN),U(NN),WKSP(NW),RPARM(12)
1607     !C       
1608     !C     SPECIFICATIONS FOR LOCAL VARIABLES
1609     !C       
1610     !      INTEGER IB1,IB2,IB3,IB4,IB5,IDGTS,IER,IERPER,ITMAX1,LOOP,N,NB,N3
1611     !      DOUBLE PRECISION BETNEW,DIGIT1,DIGIT2,PBETA,TEMP,TIME1,TIME2,TOL
1612     !C       
1613     !C *** BEGIN: ITPACK COMMON  
1614     !C       
1615     !      INTEGER IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT       
1616     !      COMMON /ITCOM1/ IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT 
1617     !C       
1618     !      LOGICAL ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD   
1619     !      COMMON /ITCOM2/ ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD     
1620     !C       
1621     !      DOUBLE PRECISION BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA,
1622     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
1623     !      COMMON /ITCOM3/ BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA, 
1624     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
1625     !C       
1626     !C *** END  : ITPACK COMMON

1911     !      SUBROUTINE RSCG (NN,IA,JA,A,RHS,U,IWKSP,NW,WKSP,IPARM,RPARM,IERR) 
1912     !C       
1913     !C     ITPACK 2C MAIN SUBROUTINE  RSCG  (REDUCED SYSTEM CONJUGATE    
1914     !C                                       GRADIENT) 
1915     !C     EACH OF THE MAIN SUBROUTINES:   
1916     !C           JCG, JSI, SOR, SSORCG, SSORSI, RSCG, RSSI     
1917     !C     CAN BE USED INDEPENDENTLY OF THE OTHERS   
1918     !C       
1919     !C ... FUNCTION:   
1920     !C       
1921     !C          THIS SUBROUTINE, RSCG, DRIVES THE  REDUCED SYSTEM CG     
1922     !C          ALGORITHM.       
1923     !C       
1924     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
1925     !C       
1926     !C          N     INPUT INTEGER.  DIMENSION OF THE MATRIX. (= NN)    
1927     !C                 IN THE RED-BLACK MATRIX.      
1928     !C          IA,JA  INPUT INTEGER VECTORS.  THE TWO INTEGER ARRAYS OF 
1929     !C                 THE SPARSE MATRIX REPRESENTATION.       
1930     !C          A      INPUT D.P. VECTOR.  THE D.P. ARRAY OF THE SPARSE  
1931     !C                 MATRIX REPRESENTATION.
1932     !C          RHS    INPUT D.P. VECTOR.  CONTAINS THE RIGHT HAND SIDE  
1933     !C                 OF THE MATRIX PROBLEM.
1934     !C          U      INPUT/OUTPUT D.P. VECTOR.  ON INPUT, U CONTAINS THE 
1935     !C                 INITIAL GUESS TO THE SOLUTION. ON OUTPUT, IT CONTAINS 
1936     !C                 THE LATEST ESTIMATE TO THE SOLUTION.    
1937     !C          IWKSP  INTEGER VECTOR WORKSPACE OF LENGTH 3*N  
1938     !C          NW     INPUT INTEGER.  LENGTH OF AVAILABLE WKSP.  ON OUTPUT, 
1939     !C                 IPARM(8) IS AMOUNT USED.      
1940     !C          WKSP   D.P. VECTOR USED FOR WORKING SPACE.  RSCG NEEDS   
1941     !C                 THIS TO BE IN LENGTH AT LEAST 
1942     !C                 N+3*NB+2*ITMAX, IF IPARM(5)=0  (SYMMETRIC STORAGE)
1943     !C                 N+3*NB+4*ITMAX, IF IPARM(5)=1  (NONSYMMETRIC STORAGE) 
1944     !C                 HERE NB IS THE ORDER OF THE BLACK SUBSYSTEM       
1945     !C          IPARM  INTEGER VECTOR OF LENGTH 12.  ALLOWS USER TO SPECIFY
1946     !C                 SOME INTEGER PARAMETERS WHICH AFFECT THE METHOD.  IF
1947     !C          RPARM  D.P. VECTOR OF LENGTH 12. ALLOWS USER TO SPECIFY SOME 
1948     !C                 D.P. PARAMETERS WHICH AFFECT THE METHOD.
1949     !C          IER    OUTPUT INTEGER. ERROR FLAG. (= IERR)    
1950     !C       
1951     !C ... RSCG SUBPROGRAM REFERENCES:     
1952     !C       
1953     !C          FROM ITPACK    BISRCH, CHGCON, DETERM, DFAULT, ECHALL,   
1954     !C                         ECHOUT, EIGVNS, EIGVSS, EQRT1S, ITERM, TIMER
1955     !C                         ITRSCG, IVFILL, PARCON, PERMAT, 
1956     !C                         PERROR, PERVEC, PMULT, PRBNDX, PRSBLK,    
1957     !C                         PRSRED, PSTOP, QSORT, SBELM, SCAL, DCOPY, 
1958     !C                         DDOT, SUM3, UNSCAL, VFILL, VOUT, WEVMW,   
1959     !C                         ZBRENT      
1960     !C          SYSTEM         DABS, DLOG10, DBLE(AMAX0), DMAX1, MOD, DSQRT
1961     !C       
1962     !C     VERSION:  ITPACK 2C (MARCH 1982)
1963     !C       
1964     !C     CODE WRITTEN BY:  DAVID KINCAID, ROGER GRIMES, JOHN RESPESS   
1965     !C                       CENTER FOR NUMERICAL ANALYSIS     
1966     !C                       UNIVERSITY OF TEXAS     
1967     !C                       AUSTIN, TX  78712       
1968     !C                       (512) 471-1242
1969     !C       
1970     !C     FOR ADDITIONAL DETAILS ON THE   
1971     !C          (A) SUBROUTINE SEE TOMS ARTICLE 1982 
1972     !C          (B) ALGORITHM  SEE CNA REPORT 150    
1973     !C       
1974     !C     BASED ON THEORY BY:  DAVID YOUNG, DAVID KINCAID, LOU HAGEMAN  
1975     !C       
1976     !C     REFERENCE THE BOOK:  APPLIED ITERATIVE METHODS      
1977     !C                          L. HAGEMAN, D. YOUNG 
1978     !C                          ACADEMIC PRESS, 1981 
1979     !C       
1980     !C     **************************************************  
1981     !C     *               IMPORTANT NOTE                   *  
1982     !C     *                                                *  
1983     !C     *      WHEN INSTALLING ITPACK ROUTINES ON A      *  
1984     !C     *  DIFFERENT COMPUTER, RESET SOME OF THE VALUES  *  
1985     !C     *  IN  SUBROUTNE DFAULT.   MOST IMPORTANT ARE    *  
1986     !C     *                                                *  
1987     !C     *   DRELPR      MACHINE RELATIVE PRECISION       *  
1988     !C     *   RPARM(1)    STOPPING CRITERION               *  
1989     !C     *                                                *  
1990     !C     *   ALSO CHANGE SYSTEM-DEPENDENT ROUTINE         *  
1991     !C     *   SECOND USED IN TIMER                         *  
1992     !C     *                                                *  
1993     !C     **************************************************  
1994     !C       
1995     !C     SPECIFICATIONS FOR ARGUMENTS    
1996     !C       
1997     !      INTEGER IA(1),JA(1),IWKSP(1),IPARM(12),NN,NW,IERR   
1998     !      DOUBLE PRECISION A(1),RHS(NN),U(NN),WKSP(NW),RPARM(12)
1999     !C       
2000     !C     SPECIFICATIONS FOR LOCAL VARIABLES
2001     !C       
2002     !      INTEGER IB1,IB2,IB3,IB4,IB5,IDGTS,IER,IERPER,ITMAX1,JB3,LOOP,N,NB,
2003     !     *   NR,NRP1,N3 
2004     !      DOUBLE PRECISION DIGIT1,DIGIT2,TEMP,TIME1,TIME2,TOL 
2005     !C       
2006     !C *** BEGIN: ITPACK COMMON  
2007     !C       
2008     !      INTEGER IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT       
2009     !      COMMON /ITCOM1/ IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT 
2010     !C       
2011     !      LOGICAL ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD   
2012     !      COMMON /ITCOM2/ ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD     
2013     !C       
2014     !      DOUBLE PRECISION BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA,
2015     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
2016     !      COMMON /ITCOM3/ BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA, 
2017     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
2018     !C       
2019     !C *** END  : ITPACK COMMON  
2020     !C       
2021     !C ... VARIABLES IN COMMON BLOCK - ITCOM1
2022     !C       
2023     !C     IN     - ITERATION NUMBER       
2024     !C     IS     - ITERATION NUMBER WHEN PARAMETERS LAST CHANGED
2025     !C     ISYM   - SYMMETRIC/NONSYMMETRIC STORAGE FORMAT SWITCH 
2026     !C     ITMAX  - MAXIMUM NUMBER OF ITERATIONS ALLOWED       
2027     !C     LEVEL  - LEVEL OF OUTPUT CONTROL SWITCH   
2028     !C     NOUT   - OUTPUT UNIT NUMBER     
2029     !C       
2030     !C ... VARIABLES IN COMMON BLOCK - ITCOM2

2328     !      SUBROUTINE RSSI (NN,IA,JA,A,RHS,U,IWKSP,NW,WKSP,IPARM,RPARM,IERR) 
2329     !C       
2330     !C     ITPACK 2C MAIN SUBROUTINE  RSSI  (REDUCED SYSTEM SEMI-ITERATIVE)
2331     !C     EACH OF THE MAIN SUBROUTINES:   
2332     !C           JCG, JSI, SOR, SSORCG, SSORSI, RSCG, RSSI     
2333     !C     CAN BE USED INDEPENDENTLY OF THE OTHERS   
2334     !C       
2335     !C ... FUNCTION:   
2336     !C       
2337     !C          THIS SUBROUTINE, RSSI, DRIVES THE  REDUCED SYSTEM SI     
2338     !C          ALGORITHM.       
2339     !C       
2340     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
2341     !C       
2342     !C          N     INPUT INTEGER.  DIMENSION OF THE MATRIX. (= NN)    
2343     !C          IA,JA  INPUT INTEGER VECTORS.  THE TWO INTEGER ARRAYS OF 
2344     !C                 THE SPARSE MATRIX REPRESENTATION.       
2345     !C          A      INPUT D.P. VECTOR.  THE D.P. ARRAY OF THE SPARSE  
2346     !C                 MATRIX REPRESENTATION.
2347     !C          RHS    INPUT D.P. VECTOR.  CONTAINS THE RIGHT HAND SIDE  
2348     !C                 OF THE MATRIX PROBLEM.
2349     !C          U      INPUT/OUTPUT D.P. VECTOR.  ON INPUT, U CONTAINS THE 
2350     !C                 INITIAL GUESS TO THE SOLUTION. ON OUTPUT, IT CONTAINS 
2351     !C                 THE LATEST ESTIMATE TO THE SOLUTION.    
2352     !C          IWKSP  INTEGER VECTOR WORKSPACE OF LENGTH 3*N  
2353     !C          NW     INPUT INTEGER.  LENGTH OF AVAILABLE WKSP.  ON OUTPUT, 
2354     !C                 IPARM(8) IS AMOUNT USED.      
2355     !C          WKSP   D.P. VECTOR USED FOR WORKING SPACE.  RSSI 
2356     !C                 NEEDS THIS TO BE IN LENGTH AT LEAST  N + NB       
2357     !C                 HERE NB IS THE ORDER OF THE BLACK SUBSYSTEM       
2358     !C          IPARM  INTEGER VECTOR OF LENGTH 12.  ALLOWS USER TO SPECIFY
2359     !C                 SOME INTEGER PARAMETERS WHICH AFFECT THE METHOD.  IF
2360     !C          RPARM  D.P. VECTOR OF LENGTH 12. ALLOWS USER TO SPECIFY SOME 
2361     !C                 D.P. PARAMETERS WHICH AFFECT THE METHOD.
2362     !C          IER     OUTPUT INTEGER.  ERROR FLAG. (= IERR)  
2363     !C       
2364     !C ... RSSI SUBPROGRAM REFERENCES:     
2365     !C       
2366     !C          FROM ITPACK    BISRCH, CHEBY, CHGSI, DFAULT, ECHALL,     
2367     !C                         ECHOUT, ITERM, TIMER, ITRSSI, IVFILL,     
2368     !C                         PARSI, PERMAT, PERROR, PERVEC, PMULT,     
2369     !C                         PRBNDX, PRSBLK, PRSRED, PSTOP, QSORT,     
2370     !C                         DAXPY, SBELM, SCAL, DCOPY, DDOT, SUM3,    
2371     !C                         TSTCHG, UNSCAL, VEVMW, VFILL, VOUT,       
2372     !C                         WEVMW       
2373     !C          SYSTEM         DABS, DLOG10, DBLE(AMAX0), DMAX1, DBLE(FLOAT),
2374     !C                         DSQRT       
2375     !C       
2376     !C     VERSION:  ITPACK 2C (MARCH 1982)
2377     !C       
2378     !C     CODE WRITTEN BY:  DAVID KINCAID, ROGER GRIMES, JOHN RESPESS   
2379     !C                       CENTER FOR NUMERICAL ANALYSIS     
2380     !C                       UNIVERSITY OF TEXAS     
2381     !C                       AUSTIN, TX  78712       
2382     !C                       (512) 471-1242
2383     !C       
2384     !C     FOR ADDITIONAL DETAILS ON THE   
2385     !C          (A) SUBROUTINE SEE TOMS ARTICLE 1982 
2386     !C          (B) ALGORITHM  SEE CNA REPORT 150    
2387     !C       
2388     !C     BASED ON THEORY BY:  DAVID YOUNG, DAVID KINCAID, LOU HAGEMAN  
2389     !C       
2390     !C     REFERENCE THE BOOK:  APPLIED ITERATIVE METHODS      
2391     !C                          L. HAGEMAN, D. YOUNG 
2392     !C                          ACADEMIC PRESS, 1981 
2393     !C       
2394     !C     **************************************************  
2395     !C     *               IMPORTANT NOTE                   *  
2396     !C     *                                                *  
2397     !C     *      WHEN INSTALLING ITPACK ROUTINES ON A      *  
2398     !C     *  DIFFERENT COMPUTER, RESET SOME OF THE VALUES  *  
2399     !C     *  IN  SUBROUTNE DFAULT.   MOST IMPORTANT ARE    *  
2400     !C     *                                                *  
2401     !C     *   DRELPR      MACHINE RELATIVE PRECISION       *  
2402     !C     *   RPARM(1)    STOPPING CRITERION               *  
2403     !C     *                                                *  
2404     !C     *   ALSO CHANGE SYSTEM-DEPENDENT ROUTINE         *  
2405     !C     *   SECOND USED IN TIMER                         *  
2406     !C     *                                                *  
2407     !C     **************************************************  
2408     !C       
2409     !C     SPECIFICATIONS FOR ARGUMENTS    
2410     !C       
2411     !      INTEGER IA(1),JA(1),IWKSP(1),IPARM(12),NN,NW,IERR   
2412     !      DOUBLE PRECISION A(1),RHS(NN),U(NN),WKSP(NW),RPARM(12)
2413     !C       
2414     !C     SPECIFICATIONS FOR LOCAL VARIABLES
2415     !C       
2416     !      INTEGER IB1,IB2,IDGTS,IER,IERPER,ITMAX1,JB3,LOOP,N,NB,NR,NRP1,N3
2417     !      DOUBLE PRECISION DIGIT1,DIGIT2,TEMP,TIME1,TIME2,TOL 
2418     !C       
2419     !C *** BEGIN: ITPACK COMMON  
2420     !C       
2421     !      INTEGER IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT       
2422     !      COMMON /ITCOM1/ IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT 
2423     !C       
2424     !      LOGICAL ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD   
2425     !      COMMON /ITCOM2/ ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD     
2426     !C

2721     !      SUBROUTINE ITJCG (NN,IA,JA,A,U,U1,D,D1,DTWD,TRI)    
2722     !C       
2723     !C ... FUNCTION:   
2724     !C       
2725     !C          THIS SUBROUTINE, ITJCG, PERFORMS ONE ITERATION OF THE    
2726     !C          JACOBI CONJUGATE GRADIENT ALGORITHM.  IT IS CALLED BY JCG. 
2727     !C       
2728     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
2729     !C       
2730     !C          N      INPUT INTEGER.  DIMENSION OF THE MATRIX. (= NN)   
2731     !C          IA,JA  INPUT INTEGER VECTORS.  CONTAINS INFORMATION DEFINING 
2732     !C                 THE SPARSE MATRIX REPRESENTATION.       
2733     !C          A      INPUT D.P. VECTOR. CONTAINS THE NONZERO VALUES OF THE 
2734     !C                 LINEAR SYSTEM.      
2735     !C          U      INPUT D.P. VECTOR.  CONTAINS THE VALUE OF THE     
2736     !C                 SOLUTION VECTOR AT THE END OF IN ITERATIONS.      
2737     !C          U1     INPUT/OUTPUT D.P. VECTOR.  ON INPUT, IT CONTAINS  
2738     !C                 THE VALUE OF THE SOLUTION AT THE END OF THE IN-1  
2739     !C                 ITERATION.  ON OUTPUT, IT WILL CONTAIN THE NEWEST 
2740     !C                 ESTIMATE FOR THE SOLUTION VECTOR.       
2741     !C          D      INPUT D.P. VECTOR.  CONTAINS THE PSEUDO-RESIDUAL  
2742     !C                 VECTOR AFTER IN ITERATIONS.   
2743     !C          D1     INPUT/OUTPUT D.P. VECTOR.  ON INPUT, D1 CONTAINS  
2744     !C                 THE PSEUDO-RESIDUAL VECTOR AFTER IN-1 ITERATIONS.  ON 
2745     !C                 OUTPUT, IT WILL CONTAIN THE NEWEST PSEUDO-RESIDUAL
2746     !C                 VECTOR.   
2747     !C          DTWD   D.P. ARRAY.  USED IN THE COMPUTATIONS OF THE      
2748     !C                 ACCELERATION PARAMETER GAMMA AND THE NEW PSEUDO-  
2749     !C                 RESIDUAL. 
2750     !C          TRI    D.P. ARRAY.  STORES THE TRIDIAGONAL MATRIX ASSOCIATED 
2751     !C                 WITH THE EIGENVALUES OF THE CONJUGATE GRADIENT    
2752     !C                 POLYNOMIAL. 
2753     !C       
2754     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR ARGUMENTS    
2755     !C       
2756     !      INTEGER IA(1),JA(1),NN
2757     !      DOUBLE PRECISION A(1),U(NN),U1(NN),D(NN),D1(NN),DTWD(NN),TRI(2,1) 
2758     !C       
2759     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR LOCAL VARIABLES
2760     !C       
2761     !      INTEGER N   
2762     !      DOUBLE PRECISION CON,C1,C2,C3,C4,DNRM,DTNRM,GAMOLD,RHOOLD,RHOTMP
2763     !      LOGICAL Q1  
2764     !C       
2765     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR FUNCTION SUBPROGRAMS   
2766     !C       
2767     !      DOUBLE PRECISION DDOT 
2768     !C       
2769     !C *** BEGIN: ITPACK COMMON  
2770     !C       
2771     !      INTEGER IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT       
2772     !      COMMON /ITCOM1/ IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT 
2773     !C       
2774     !      LOGICAL ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD   
2775     !      COMMON /ITCOM2/ ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD     
2776     !C       
2777     !      DOUBLE PRECISION BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA,
2778     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
2779     !      COMMON /ITCOM3/ BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA, 
2780     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
2781     !C       
2782     !C *** END  : ITPACK COMMON  
2783     !C       
2784     !C     DESCRIPTION OF VARIABLES IN COMMON BLOCKS IN SUBROUTINE JCG   
2785     !C       
2786     !C ... COMPUTE NEW ESTIMATE FOR CME IF ADAPT = .TRUE.      
2787     !C       
2788     !      IF (ADAPT) CALL CHGCON (TRI,GAMOLD,RHOOLD,1)
2789     !C

2791     !C

2822     !      SUBROUTINE ITJSI (NN,IA,JA,A,RHS,U,U1,D,ICNT)       
2823     !C       
2824     !C ... FUNCTION:   
2825     !C       
2826     !C          THIS SUBROUTINE, ITJSI, PERFORMS ONE ITERATION OF THE    
2827     !C          JACOBI SEMI-ITERATIVE ALGORITHM.  IT IS CALLED BY JSI.   
2828     !C       
2829     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:

3574     !      INTEGER FUNCTION BISRCH (N,K,L) 
3575     !C       
3576     !C ... BISRCH IS AN INTEGER FUNCTION WHICH USES A BISECTION SEARCH   
3577     !C     TO FIND THE ENTRY J IN THE ARRAY K SUCH THAT THE VALUE L IS   
3578     !C     GREATER THAN OR EQUAL TO K(J) AND STRICTLY LESS THAN K(J+1).  
3579     !C       
3580     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
3581     !C       
3582     !C          N      INTEGER LENGTH OF VECTOR K    
3583     !C          K      INTEGER VECTOR      
3584     !C          L      INTEGER CONSTANT SUCH THAT  K(J) .GE. L .LT. K(J+1) 
3585     !C                 WITH J RETURNED AS VALUE OF INTEGER FUNCTION BISRCH 
3586     !C       
3587     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR ARGUMENTS    
3588     !C       
3589     !      INTEGER N,L,K(N)      
3590     !C       
3591     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR LOCAL VARIABLES
3592     !C       
3593     !      INTEGER JLEFT,JMID,JRIGHT       
3594     !C       
3595     !      JLEFT = 1   
3596     !      JRIGHT = N  
3597     !      IF (N.EQ.2) GO TO 40  
3598     !      JMID = (N+1)/2
3599     !C       
3600     !   10 IF (L.GE.K(JMID)) GO TO 20      
3601     !C       
3602     !C ...... L .GE. K(LEFT)  AND  L .LT. K(JMID)    
3603     !C       
3604     !      JRIGHT = JMID 
3605     !      GO TO 30    
3606     !C       
3607     !C ...... L .GE. K(JMID)  AND  L .LT. K(JRIGHT)  
3608     !C       
3609     !   20 JLEFT = JMID
3610     !C       
3611     !C ...... TEST FOR CONVERGENCE 
3612     !C       
3613     !   30 IF (JRIGHT-JLEFT.EQ.1) GO TO 40 
3614     !      JMID = JLEFT+(JRIGHT-JLEFT+1)/2 
3615     !      GO TO 10    
3616     !C       
3617     !C ...... BISECTION SEARCH FINISHED    
3618     !C       
3619     !   40 BISRCH = JLEFT
3620     !C       
3621     !      RETURN      
3622     !      END 
3623     !      DOUBLE PRECISION FUNCTION CHEBY (QA,QT,RRR,IP,CME,SME)
3624     !C       
3625     !C     COMPUTES THE SOLUTION TO THE CHEBYSHEV EQUATION     
3626     !C       
3627     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
3628     !C       
3629     !C          QA     RATIO OF PSEUDO-RESIDUALS     
3630     !C          QT     VIRTUAL SPECTRAL RADIUS       
3631     !C          RRR    ADAPTIVE PARAMETER  
3632     !C          IP     NUMBER OF ITERATIONS SINCE LAST CHANGE OF 
3633     !C                     PARAMETERS      
3634     !C          CME,   ESTIMATES FOR THE LARGEST AND SMALLEST EIGEN-     
3635     !C          SME      VALUES OF THE ITERATION MATRIX
3636     !C       
3637     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR ARGUMENTS    
3638     !C       
3639     !      INTEGER IP  
3640     !      DOUBLE PRECISION CME,QA,QT,RRR,SME
3641     !C       
3642     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR LOCAL VARIABLES
3643     !C       
3644     !      DOUBLE PRECISION X,Y,Z
3645     !C       
3646     !      Z = .5D0*(QA+DSQRT(DABS(QA**2-QT**2)))*(1.D0+RRR**IP) 
3647     !      X = Z**(1.D0/DBLE(FLOAT(IP)))   
3648     !      Y = (X+RRR/X)/(1.D0+RRR)
3649     !C       
3650     !      CHEBY = .5D0*(CME+SME+Y*(2.D0-CME-SME))   
3651     !C       
3652     !      RETURN      
3653     !      END 
3654     !      SUBROUTINE CHGCON (TRI,GAMOLD,RHOOLD,IBMTH) 
3655     !C       
3656     !C     COMPUTES THE NEW ESTIMATE FOR THE LARGEST EIGENVALUE FOR      
3657     !C     CONJUGATE GRADIENT ACCELERATION.
3658     !C       
3659     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
3660     !C       
3661     !C          TRI    TRIDIAGONAL MATRIX ASSOCIATED WITH THE EIGENVALUES
3662     !C                    OF THE CONJUGATE GRADIENT POLYNOMIAL 
3663     !C          GAMOLD 
3664     !C            AND  
3665     !C          RHOOLD PREVIOUS VALUES OF ACCELERATION PARAMETERS
3666     !C          IBMTH  INDICATOR OF BASIC METHOD BEING ACCELERATED BY CG 
3667     !C                      IBMTH = 1,  JACOBI       
3668     !C                            = 2,  REDUCED SYSTEM 
3669     !C                            = 3,  SSOR 
3670     !C       
3671     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR ARGUMENTS    
3672     !C       
3673     !      INTEGER IBMTH 
3674     !      DOUBLE PRECISION TRI(2,1),GAMOLD,RHOOLD   
3675     !C       
3676     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR LOCAL VARIABLES
3677     !C       
3678     !      INTEGER IB2,IB3,IER,IP
3679     !      DOUBLE PRECISION CMOLD,END,START,EIGVSS,EIGVNS      
3680     !C       
3681     !C *** BEGIN: ITPACK COMMON  
3682     !C       
3683     !      INTEGER IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT       
3684     !      COMMON /ITCOM1/ IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT 
3685     !C       
3686     !      LOGICAL ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD   
3687     !      COMMON /ITCOM2/ ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD     
3688     !C       
3689     !      DOUBLE PRECISION BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA,
3690     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
3691     !      COMMON /ITCOM3/ BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA, 
3692     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
3693     !C

4148     !      DO 80 I = 1,NS,INCX   
4149     !         DY(I) = DX(I)      
4150     !   80 CONTINUE    
4151     !      RETURN      
4152     !      END 
4153     !      DOUBLE PRECISION FUNCTION DDOT (N,DX,INCX,DY,INCY)  
4154     !C       
4155     !C     RETURNS THE DOT PRODUCT OF DOUBLE PRECISION DX AND DY.
4156     !C       
4157     !      DOUBLE PRECISION DX(1),DY(1)    
4158     !      DDOT = 0.D0 
4159     !      IF (N.LE.0) RETURN    
4160     !      IF (INCX.EQ.INCY) IF (INCX-1) 10 , 30 , 70
4161     !   10 CONTINUE    
4162     !C       
4163     !C         CODE FOR UNEQUAL OR NONPOSITIVE INCREMENTS.     
4164     !C       
4165     !      IX = 1      
4166     !      IY = 1      
4167     !      IF (INCX.LT.0) IX = (-N+1)*INCX+1 
4168     !      IF (INCY.LT.0) IY = (-N+1)*INCY+1 
4169     !      DO 20 I = 1,N 
4170     !         DDOT = DDOT+DX(IX)*DY(IY)    
4171     !         IX = IX+INCX       
4172     !         IY = IY+INCY       
4173     !   20 CONTINUE    
4174     !      RETURN      
4175     !C       
4176     !C        CODE FOR BOTH INCREMENTS EQUAL TO 1.   
4177     !C       
4178     !C        CLEAN-UP LOOP SO REMAINING VECTOR LENGTH IS A MULTIPLE OF 5. 
4179     !C       
4180     !   30 M = N-(N/5)*5 
4181     !      IF (M.EQ.0) GO TO 50  
4182     !      DO 40 I = 1,M 
4183     !         DDOT = DDOT+DX(I)*DY(I)      
4184     !   40 CONTINUE    
4185     !      IF (N.LT.5) RETURN    
4186     !   50 MP1 = M+1   
4187     !      DO 60 I = MP1,N,5     
4188     !         DDOT = DDOT+DX(I)*DY(I)+DX(I+1)*DY(I+1)+DX(I+2)*DY(I+2)+DX(I+3)
4189     !     *      *DY(I+3)+DX(I+4)*DY(I+4)  
4190     !   60 CONTINUE    
4191     !      RETURN      
4192     !C       
4193     !C         CODE FOR POSITIVE EQUAL INCREMENTS .NE.1.       
4194     !C       
4195     !   70 CONTINUE    
4196     !      NS = N*INCX 
4197     !      DO 80 I = 1,NS,INCX   
4198     !         DDOT = DDOT+DX(I)*DY(I)      
4199     !   80 CONTINUE    
4200     !      RETURN      
4201     !      END 
4202     !      DOUBLE PRECISION FUNCTION DETERM (N,TRI,XLMDA)      
4203     !C       
4204     !C     THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTES THE DETERMINANT OF A SYMMETRIC       
4205     !C     TRIDIAGONAL MATRIX GIVEN BY TRI. DET(TRI - XLMDA*I) = 0       
4206     !C       
4207     !C ... PARAMETER LIST
4208     !C       
4209     !C          N      ORDER OF TRIDIAGONAL SYSTEM   
4210     !C          TRI    SYMMETRIC TRIDIAGONAL MATRIX OF ORDER N 
4211     !C          XLMDA  ARGUMENT FOR CHARACTERISTIC EQUATION    
4212     !C       
4213     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR ARGUMENTS    
4214     !C       
4215     !      INTEGER N   
4216     !      DOUBLE PRECISION TRI(2,1),XLMDA 
4217     !C       
4218     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR LOCAL VARIABLES
4219     !C       
4220     !      INTEGER ICNT,L,NM1    
4221     !      DOUBLE PRECISION D1,D2,D3       
4222     !C       
4223     !      NM1 = N-1   
4224     !      D2 = TRI(1,N)-XLMDA   
4225     !      D1 = D2*(TRI(1,NM1)-XLMDA)-TRI(2,N)       
4226     !      IF (N.EQ.2) GO TO 20  
4227     !C       
4228     !C ... BEGINNING OF LOOP     
4229     !C       
4230     !      DO 10 ICNT = 2,NM1    
4231     !         L = NM1-ICNT+2     
4232     !         D3 = D2  
4233     !         D2 = D1  
4234     !         D1 = (TRI(1,L-1)-XLMDA)*D2-D3*TRI(2,L) 
4235     !   10 CONTINUE    
4236     !C       
4237     !C ... DETERMINANT COMPUTED  
4238     !C       
4239     !   20 DETERM = D1 
4240     !C       
4241     !      RETURN      
4242     !      END 
4243     !      SUBROUTINE DFAULT (IPARM,RPARM) 
4244     !C       
4245     !C ... THIS SUBROUTINE SETS THE DEFAULT VALUES OF IPARM AND RPARM.   
4246     !C       
4247     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
4248     !C       
4249     !C          IPARM  
4250     !C           AND   
4251     !C          RPARM  ARRAYS SPECIFYING OPTIONS AND TOLERANCES
4252     !C       
4253     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR ARGUMENTS    
4254     !C       
4255     !      INTEGER IPARM(12)     
4256     !      DOUBLE PRECISION RPARM(12)      
4257     !C       
4258     !C *** BEGIN: ITPACK COMMON  
4259     !C       
4260     !      INTEGER IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT       
4261     !      COMMON /ITCOM1/ IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT 
4262     !C       
4263     !      LOGICAL ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD   
4264     !      COMMON /ITCOM2/ ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD     
4265     !C       
4266     !      DOUBLE PRECISION BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA,
4267     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
4268     !      COMMON /ITCOM3/ BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA, 
4269     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
4270     !C       
4271     !C *** END  : ITPACK COMMON  
4272     !C       
4273     !C     DESCRIPTION OF VARIABLES IN COMMON BLOCKS IN MAIN SUBROUTINE  
4274     !C       
4275     !C     DRELPR  - COMPUTER PRECISION (APPROX.)    
4276     !C     IF INSTALLER OF PACKAGE DOES NOT KNOW DRELPR VALUE, 
4277     !C     AN APPROXIMATE VALUE CAN BE DETERMINED FROM A SIMPLE
4278     !C     FORTRAN PROGRAM SUCH AS 
4279     !C       
4280     !C     DOUBLE PRECISION DRELPR, TEMP   
4281     !C     DRELPR = 1.0D0
4282     !C   2 DRELPR = 0.5D0*DRELPR 
4283     !C     TEMP = DRELPR + 1.0D0 
4284     !C     IF(TEMP .GT. 1.0D0)  GO TO 2    
4285     !C     WRITE(6,3) DRELPR     
4286     !C   3 FORMAT(5X,D15.8)      
4287     !C     STOP
4288     !C     END 
4289     !C       
4290     !C     SOME VALUES ARE:      
4291     !C       
4292     !C     DRELPR = 1.26D-29  FOR CDC CYBER 170/750  (APPROX.) 2**-96    
4293     !C            = 2.22D-16  FOR DEC 10             (APPROX.) 2**-52    
4294     !C            = 7.11D-15  FOR VAX 11/780         (APPROX.) 2**-47    
4295     !C            = 1.14D-13  FOR IBM 370/158        (APPROX.) 2**-43    
4296     !C       
4297     !C             *** SHOULD BE CHANGED FOR OTHER MACHINES ***
4298     !C       
4299     !C     TO FACILITATE CONVERGENCE, RPARM(1) SHOULD BE SET TO
4300     !C          500.*DRELPR OR LARGER      
4301     !C       
4302     !      DRELPR = 7.11D-15
4303     !C       
4304     !      IPARM(1) = 100
4305     !      IPARM(2) = 0
4306     !      IPARM(3) = 0
4307     !      IPARM(4) = 6
4308     !      IPARM(5) = 0
4309     !      IPARM(6) = 1
4310     !      IPARM(7) = 1
4311     !      IPARM(8) = 0
4312     !      IPARM(9) = -1 
4313     !      IPARM(10) = 0 
4314     !      IPARM(11) = 0 
4315     !      IPARM(12) = 0 
4316     !C       
4317     !      RPARM(1) = 0.5D-5     
4318     !      RPARM(2) = 0.D0       
4319     !      RPARM(3) = 0.D0       
4320     !      RPARM(4) = .75D0      
4321     !      RPARM(5) = 1.D0       
4322     !      RPARM(6) = 0.D0       
4323     !      RPARM(7) = .25D0      
4324     !      RPARM(8) = 1.D2*DRELPR
4325     !      RPARM(9) = 0.D0       
4326     !      RPARM(10) = 0.D0      
4327     !      RPARM(11) = 0.D0      
4328     !      RPARM(12) = 0.D0      
4329     !C       
4330     !      RETURN      
4331     !      END 
4332     !      SUBROUTINE ECHALL (NN,IA,JA,A,RHS,IPARM,RPARM,ICALL)
4333     !C

4335     !C ... INFORMATION CONTAINED IN IPARM AND RPARM. ECHALL ALSO PRINTS THE
4336     !C ... VALUES OF ALL THE PARAMETERS IN IPARM AND RPARM.

4339     !C

4343     !C                    TOLERANCES

4367     !      COMMON /ITCOM3/ BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA, 
4368     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
4369     !C       
4370     !C *** END  : ITPACK COMMON  
4371     !C       
4372     !C     DESCRIPTION OF VARIABLES IN COMMON BLOCKS IN MAIN SUBROUTINE  
4373     !C       
4374     !      IF (ICALL.NE.1) GO TO 100       
4375     !      N = NN      
4376     !      NP1 = N+1   
4377     !      NZRO = IA(NP1)-1      
4378     !C       
4379     !C ... INITIALIZE ITPACK COMMON
4380     !C       
4381     !      ZETA = RPARM(1)       
4382     !      CME = RPARM(2)
4383     !      SME = RPARM(3)
4384     !      FF = RPARM(4) 
4385     !      OMEGA = RPARM(5)      
4386     !      SPECR = RPARM(6)

4389     !      LEVEL = IPARM(2)      
4390     !      ISYM = IPARM(5)       
4391     !C       
4392     !      ADAPT = .FALSE.       
4393     !      PARTAD = .FALSE.      
4394     !      BETADT = .FALSE.      
4395     !      IF (IPARM(6).EQ.1.OR.IPARM(6).EQ.3) ADAPT = .TRUE.  
4396     !      IF (IPARM(6).EQ.1) BETADT = .TRUE.
4397     !      IF (IPARM(6).EQ.2) PARTAD = .TRUE.
4398     !C       
4399     !      CASEII = .FALSE.      
4400     !      IF (IPARM(7).EQ.2) CASEII = .TRUE.
4401     !      IF (CASEII) SME = -CME
4402     !      IF (.NOT.CASEII.AND.SME.EQ.0.D0) SME = -1.D0
4403     !      SPR = SME   
4404     !C       
4405     !C ... SET REST OF COMMON VARIABLES TO ZERO      
4406     !C       
4407     !      IN = 0      
4408     !      IS = 0      
4409     !      HALT = .FALSE.
4410     !      BDELNM = 0.D0 
4411     !      DELNNM = 0.D0 
4412     !      DELSNM = 0.D0 
4413     !      GAMMA = 0.D0
4414     !      QA = 0.D0   
4415     !      QT = 0.D0   
4416     !      RHO = 0.D0  
4417     !      RRR = 0.D0  
4418     !      SIGE = 0.D0 
4419     !      STPTST = 0.D0 
4420     !      UDNM = 0.D0 
4421     !C

4440     !      WRITE (NOUT,70)       
4441     !   70 FORMAT (/2X,'RHS ARRAY')
4442     !      WRITE (NOUT,60) (RHS(I),I=1,N)  
4443     !   80 WRITE (NOUT,90)       
4444     !   90 FORMAT (///30X,'INITIAL ITERATIVE PARAMETERS')      
4445     !      GO TO 120   
4446     !  100 WRITE (NOUT,110)      
4447     !  110 FORMAT (///30X,'FINAL ITERATIVE PARAMETERS')
4448     !  120 WRITE (NOUT,130) IPARM(1),LEVEL,IPARM(3),NOUT,ISYM,IPARM(6)

4473     !      SUBROUTINE ECHOUT (IPARM,RPARM,IMTHD)     
4474     !C       
4475     !C     THIS ROUTINE INITIALIZES THE ITPACK COMMON BLOCKS FROM THE    
4476     !C     INFORMATION CONTAINED IN IPARM AND RPARM. 
4477     !C       
4478     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
4479     !C       
4480     !C          IPARM  
4481     !C           AND   
4482     !C          RPARM  ARRAYS OF PARAMETERS SPECIFYING OPTIONS AND       
4483     !C                    TOLERANCES       
4484     !C          IMTHD  INDICATOR OF METHOD 
4485     !C                    IMTHD = 1,  JCG  
4486     !C                    IMTHD = 2,  JSI  
4487     !C                    IMTHD = 3,  SOR  
4488     !C                    IMTHD = 4,  SSORCG 
4489     !C                    IMTHD = 5,  SSORSI 
4490     !C                    IMTHD = 6,  RSCG 
4491     !C                    IMTHD = 7,  RSSI 
4492     !C       
4493     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR ARGUMENTS    
4494     !C       
4495     !      INTEGER IPARM(12),IMTHD 
4496     !      DOUBLE PRECISION RPARM(12)      
4497     !C       
4498     !C *** BEGIN: ITPACK COMMON  
4499     !C       
4500     !      INTEGER IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT       
4501     !      COMMON /ITCOM1/ IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT 
4502     !C       
4503     !      LOGICAL ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD   
4504     !      COMMON /ITCOM2/ ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD     
4505     !C       
4506     !      DOUBLE PRECISION BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA,
4507     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
4508     !      COMMON /ITCOM3/ BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA, 
4509     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
4510     !C       
4511     !C *** END  : ITPACK COMMON  
4512     !C       
4513     !C     DESCRIPTION OF VARIABLES IN COMMON BLOCKS IN MAIN SUBROUTINE  
4514     !C       
4515     !C ... INITIALIZE ITPACK COMMON
4516     !C       
4517     !      ZETA = RPARM(1)       
4518     !      CME = RPARM(2)
4519     !      SME = RPARM(3)

4523     !      BETAB = RPARM(7)      
4524     !      ITMAX = IPARM(1)      
4525     !      LEVEL = IPARM(2)      
4526     !      ISYM = IPARM(5)       
4527     !C       
4528     !      ADAPT = .FALSE.       
4529     !      PARTAD = .FALSE.      
4530     !      BETADT = .FALSE.      
4531     !      IF (IPARM(6).EQ.1.OR.IPARM(6).EQ.3) ADAPT = .TRUE.  
4532     !      IF (IPARM(6).EQ.1) BETADT = .TRUE.
4533     !      IF (IPARM(6).EQ.2) PARTAD = .TRUE.
4534     !C       
4535     !      CASEII = .FALSE.      
4536     !      IF (IPARM(7).EQ.2) CASEII = .TRUE.
4537     !      IF (CASEII) SME = -CME
4538     !      IF (.NOT.CASEII.AND.SME.EQ.0.D0) SME = -1.D0
4539     !      SPR = SME   
4540     !C       
4541     !C ... SET REST OF COMMON VARIABLES TO ZERO      
4542     !C       
4543     !      IN = 0      
4544     !      IS = 0      
4545     !      HALT = .FALSE.
4546     !      BDELNM = 0.D0 
4547     !      DELNNM = 0.D0 
4548     !      DELSNM = 0.D0 
4549     !      GAMMA = 0.D0
4550     !      QA = 0.D0   
4551     !      QT = 0.D0   
4552     !      RHO = 0.D0  
4553     !      RRR = 0.D0  
4554     !      SIGE = 0.D0 
4555     !      STPTST = 0.D0 
4556     !      UDNM = 0.D0 
4557     !      IF (LEVEL.LE.2) RETURN

4560     !C     ITERATIVE PARAMETERS  
4561     !C       
4562     !      WRITE (NOUT,10) ISYM,ITMAX,ZETA,ADAPT,CASEII
4563     !   10 FORMAT (///30X,'INITIAL ITERATIVE PARAMETERS',3X,   
4564     !     *   'RELEVANT SWITCHES'/35X,'ISYM   =',I15,8X,'IPARM(5)'/35X,  
4565     !     *   'ITMAX  =',I15,8X,'IPARM(1)'/35X,'ZETA   =',D15.8,8X,'RPARM(1)'
4566     !     *   /35X,'ADAPT  =',L15,8X,'IPARM(6)'/35X,'CASEII =',L15,8X,   
4567     !     *   'IPARM(7)')
4568     !      GO TO (80,20,100,60,40,80,20), IMTHD      
4569     !C       
4570     !C ... JSI, RSSI   
4571     !C       
4572     !   20 WRITE (NOUT,30) FF,CME,SME      
4573     !   30 FORMAT (35X,'FF     =',D15.8,8X,'RPARM(4)'/35X,'CME    =',D15.8,8X
4574     !     *   ,'RPARM(2)'/35X,'SME    =',D15.8,8X,'RPARM(3)'///) 
4575     !      RETURN      
4576     !C       
4577     !C ... SSORSI      
4578     !C

4605     !      DOUBLE PRECISION FUNCTION EIGVNS (N,TRI,D,E2,IER)   
4606     !C       
4607     !C     COMPUTES THE LARGEST EIGENVALUE OF A SYMMETRIC TRIDIAGONAL MATRIX 
4608     !C     FOR CONJUGATE GRADIENT ACCELERATION.      
4609     !C       
4610     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
4611     !C       
4612     !C          N      ORDER OF TRIDIAGONAL SYSTEM   
4613     !C          TRI    SYMMETRIC TRIDIAGONAL MATRIX OF ORDER N 
4614     !C          D      ARRAY FOR EQRT1S (NEGATIVE DIAGONAL ELEMENTS)     
4615     !C          E2     ARRAY FOR EQRT1S (SUPER DIAGONAL ELEMENTS)
4616     !C          IER    ERROR FLAG: ON RETURN, IER=0 INDICATES THAT       
4617     !C                    THE LARGEST EIGENVALUE OF TRI WAS FOUND.       
4618     !C       
4619     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR ARGUMENTS

4625     !C

4627     !C       
4628     !      EIGVNS = 0.D0 
4629     !C       
4630     !      D(1) = -TRI(1,1)      
4631     !      DO 10 I = 2,N 
4632     !         D(I) = -TRI(1,I)   
4633     !         E2(I) = DABS(TRI(2,I))       
4634     !   10 CONTINUE

4636     !      CALL EQRT1S (D,E2,N,1,0,IER)

4641     !      DOUBLE PRECISION FUNCTION EIGVSS (N,TRI,START,ZETA,ITMAX,IER)

4680     !      SUBROUTINE EQRT1S (D,E2,NN,M,ISW,IERR)    
4681     !C       
4682     !C   MODIFIED IMSL ROUTINE NAME   - EQRT1S       
4683     !C       
4684     !C-----------------------------------------------------------------------
4685     !C       
4686     !C   COMPUTER            - CDC/SINGLE  
4687     !C       
4688     !C   LATEST REVISION     - JUNE 1, 1980
4689     !C       
4690     !C   PURPOSE             - SMALLEST OR LARGEST M EIGENVALUES OF A    
4691     !C                           SYMMETRIC TRIDIAGONAL MATRIX  
4692     !C       
4693     !C   USAGE               - CALL EQRT1S (D,E2,N,M,ISW,IER)  
4694     !C       
4695     !C   ARGUMENTS    D      - INPUT VECTOR OF LENGTH N CONTAINING       
4696     !C                           THE DIAGONAL ELEMENTS OF THE MATRIX.  THE 
4697     !C                           COMPUTED EIGENVALUES REPLACE THE FIRST M
4698     !C                           COMPONENTS OF THE VECTOR D IN NON-      
4699     !C                           DECREASING SEQUENCE, WHILE THE REMAINING
4700     !C                           COMPONENTS ARE LOST.
4701     !C                E2     - INPUT VECTOR OF LENGTH N CONTAINING       
4702     !C                           THE SQUARES OF THE OFF-DIAGONAL ELEMENTS
4703     !C                           OF THE MATRIX.  INPUT E2 IS DESTROYED.  
4704     !C                N      - INPUT SCALAR CONTAINING THE ORDER OF THE  
4705     !C                           MATRIX. (= NN)      
4706     !C                M      - INPUT SCALAR CONTAINING THE NUMBER OF     
4707     !C                           SMALLEST EIGENVALUES DESIRED (M IS      
4708     !C                           LESS THAN OR EQUAL TO N).     
4709     !C                ISW    - INPUT SCALAR MEANING AS FOLLOWS - 
4710     !C                           ISW=1 MEANS THAT THE MATRIX IS KNOWN TO BE
4711     !C                             POSITIVE DEFINITE.
4712     !C                           ISW=0 MEANS THAT THE MATRIX IS NOT KNOWN
4713     !C                             TO BE POSITIVE DEFINITE.    
4714     !C                IER    - ERROR PARAMETER. (OUTPUT) (= IERR)
4715     !C                           WARNING ERROR       
4716     !C                             IER = 601 INDICATES THAT SUCCESSIVE   
4717     !C                               ITERATES TO THE K-TH EIGENVALUE WERE NOT
4718     !C                               MONOTONE INCREASING. THE VALUE K IS 
4719     !C                               STORED IN E2(1).
4720     !C                           TERMINAL ERROR      
4721     !C                             IER = 602 INDICATES THAT ISW=1 BUT MATRIX 
4722     !C                               IS NOT POSITIVE DEFINITE  
4723     !C       
4724     !C   PRECISION/HARDWARE  - SINGLE AND DOUBLE/H32 
4725     !C                       - SINGLE/H36,H48,H60    
4726     !C       
4727     !C   NOTATION            - INFORMATION ON SPECIAL NOTATION AND       
4728     !C                           CONVENTIONS IS AVAILABLE IN THE MANUAL  
4729     !C                           INTRODUCTION OR THROUGH IMSL ROUTINE UHELP
4730     !C       
4731     !C   REMARKS      AS WRITTEN, THE ROUTINE COMPUTES THE M SMALLEST    
4732     !C                EIGENVALUES. TO COMPUTE THE M LARGEST EIGENVALUES, 
4733     !C                REVERSE THE SIGN OF EACH ELEMENT OF D BEFORE AND   
4734     !C                AFTER CALLING THE ROUTINE. IN THIS CASE, ISW MUST  
4735     !C                EQUAL ZERO.
4736     !C       
4737     !C   COPYRIGHT           - 1980 BY IMSL, INC. ALL RIGHTS RESERVED.   
4738     !C       
4739     !C   WARRANTY            - IMSL WARRANTS ONLY THAT IMSL TESTING HAS BEEN 
4740     !C                           APPLIED TO THIS CODE. NO OTHER WARRANTY,
4741     !C                           EXPRESSED OR IMPLIED, IS APPLICABLE.    
4742     !C       
4743     !C-----------------------------------------------------------------------
4744     !C       
4745     !C *** BEGIN: ITPACK COMMON  
4746     !C       
4747     !      INTEGER IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT       
4748     !      COMMON /ITCOM1/ IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT 
4749     !C       
4750     !      LOGICAL ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD   
4751     !      COMMON /ITCOM2/ ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD     
4752     !C       
4753     !      DOUBLE PRECISION BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA,
4754     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
4755     !      COMMON /ITCOM3/ BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA, 
4756     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
4757     !C       
4758     !C *** END  : ITPACK COMMON  
4759     !C

4928     !      SUBROUTINE ITERM (NN,A,U,WK,IMTHDD)       
4929     !C       
4930     !C     THIS ROUTINE PRODUCES THE ITERATION SUMMARY LINE AT THE END   
4931     !C     OF EACH ITERATION. IF LEVEL = 5, THE LATEST APPROXIMATION     
4932     !C     TO THE SOLUTION WILL BE PRINTED.
4933     !C       
4934     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
4935     !C       
4936     !C          NN     ORDER OF SYSTEM OR, FOR REDUCED SYSTEM  
4937     !C                    ROUTINES, ORDER OF BLACK SUBSYSTEM   
4938     !C          A      ITERATION MATRIX    
4939     !C          U      SOLUTION ESTIMATE   
4940     !C          WK     WORK ARRAY OF LENGTH NN       
4941     !C          IMTHD  INDICATOR OF METHOD (=IMTHDD) 
4942     !C                    IMTHD = 1,  JCG  
4943     !C                    IMTHD = 2,  JSI  
4944     !C                    IMTHD = 3,  SOR  
4945     !C                    IMTHD = 4,  SSORCG

4954     !C       
4955     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR LOCAL VARIABLES
4956     !C       
4957     !      INTEGER I,IMTHDD,IP,N 
4958     !      DOUBLE PRECISION QTFF 
4959     !C

4976     !      IMTHD = IMTHDD

4979     !C       
4980     !      IF (LEVEL.LT.2) RETURN
4981     !      GO TO (10,110,170,210,50,10,110), IMTHD   
4982     !   10 IF (IN.GT.0) GO TO 30 
4983     !C       
4984     !C ... PRINT HEADER FOR JCG AND RSCG   
4985     !C

4987     !   20 FORMAT (////15X,'INTERMEDIATE OUTPUT AFTER EACH ITERATION'//

4995     !      IF (LEVEL.GE.4) GO TO 250       
4996     !C

5367     !      SUBROUTINE PARCON (DTNRM,C1,C2,C3,C4,GAMOLD,RHOTMP,IBMTH)

5409     !C *** END  : ITPACK COMMON

5538     !      DOUBLE PRECISION FUNCTION PBETA (NN,IA,JA,A,V,W1,W2)

5645     !      SUBROUTINE PBSOR (NN,IA,JA,A,U,RHS)       
5646     !C       
5647     !C     ... THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTES A BACKWARD SOR SWEEP.  
5648     !C       
5649     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
5650     !C       
5651     !C          N      ORDER OF SYSTEM (= NN)
5652     !C          OMEGA  RELAXATION FACTOR   
5653     !C          IA,JA  INTEGER ARRAYS OF SPARSE MATRIX REPRESENTATION    
5654     !C          A      D.P. ARRAY OF SPARSE MATRIX REPRESENTATION
5655     !C          U      LATEST ESTIMATE OF SOLUTION   
5656     !C          RHS    RIGHT HAND SIDE OF MATRIX PROBLEM       
5657     !C       
5658     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR ARGUMENTS    
5659     !C       
5660     !      INTEGER IA(1),JA(1),NN
5661     !      DOUBLE PRECISION A(1),U(NN),RHS(NN)       
5662     !C       
5663     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR LOCAL VARIABLES
5664     !C

5666     !      DOUBLE PRECISION OMM1,SUM,UI    
5667     !C       
5668     !C *** BEGIN: ITPACK COMMON  
5669     !C       
5670     !      INTEGER IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT       
5671     !      COMMON /ITCOM1/ IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT 
5672     !C       
5673     !      LOGICAL ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD   
5674     !      COMMON /ITCOM2/ ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD     
5675     !C       
5676     !      DOUBLE PRECISION BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA,
5677     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
5678     !      COMMON /ITCOM3/ BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA, 
5679     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
5680     !C       
5681     !C *** END  : ITPACK COMMON  
5682     !C       
5683     !C     DESCRIPTION OF VARIABLES IN COMMON BLOCK IN MAIN SUBROUTINE   
5684     !C       
5685     !      N = NN      
5686     !      NPL1 = N+1  
5687     !      OMM1 = OMEGA-1.D0     
5688     !      IF (ISYM.EQ.0) GO TO 40 
5689     !C       
5690     !C     *************** NON - SYMMETRIC SECTION **********************
5691     !C       
5692     !      DO 30 I = 1,N 
5693     !         II = NPL1-I
5694     !         IBGN = IA(II)      
5695     !         IEND = IA(II+1)-1

5697     !         IF (IBGN.GT.IEND) GO TO 20   
5698     !         DO 10 JJ = IBGN,IEND 
5699     !            JAJJ = JA(JJ)   
5700     !            SUM = SUM-A(JJ)*U(JAJJ)   
5701     !   10    CONTINUE 
5702     !   20    U(II) = OMEGA*SUM-OMM1*U(II) 
5703     !   30 CONTINUE    
5704     !      RETURN

5727     !            SUM = SUM-A(JJ)*U(JAJJ)
