5734     !      SUBROUTINE PERMAT (NN,IA,JA,A,P,NEWIA,ISYM,LEVEL,NOUT,IERR)   
5735     !C       
5736     !C*********************************************************************
5737     !C       
5738     !C ... SUBROUTINE PERMAT TAKES THE SPARSE MATRIX REPRESENTATION      
5739     !C     OF THE MATRIX STORED IN THE ARRAYS IA, JA, AND A AND
5740     !C     PERMUTES BOTH ROWS AND COLUMNS OVERWRITING THE PREVIOUS       
5741     !C     STRUCTURE.  
5742     !C       
5743     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
5744     !C       
5745     !C         N      ORDER OF SYSTEM (= NN) 
5746     !C         IA,JA  INTEGER ARRAYS OF THE SPARSE MATRIX REPRESENTATION 
5747     !C         A      D.P. ARRAY OF THE SPARSE MATRIX REPRESENTATION     
5748     !C         P      PERMUTATION VECTOR   
5749     !C         NEWIA  INTEGER WORK VECTOR OF LENGTH N
5750     !C         ISYM   SYMMETRIC/NONSYMMETRIC STORAGE SWITCH    
5751     !C         LEVEL  SWITCH CONTROLLING LEVEL OF OUTPUT       
5752     !C         NOUT OUTPUT UNIT NUMBER     
5753     !C         IER    OUTPUT ERROR FLAG (= IERR)     
5754     !C       
5755     !C                   IER =   0  NORMAL RETURN    
5756     !C                   IER = 301  NO ENTRY IN ITH ROW OF ORIGINAL      
5757     !C                              MATRIX. IF LEVEL IS GREATER THAN     
5758     !C                              0, I WILL BE PRINTED       
5759     !C                   IER = 302  THERE IS NO ENTRY IN THE ITH ROW     
5760     !C                              OF THE PERMUTED MATRIX     
5761     !C                   IER = 303  ERROR RETURN FROM QSORT IN 
5762     !C                              SORTING THE ITH ROW OF THE 
5763     !C                              PERMUTED MATRIX  
5764     !C ... IT IS ASSUMED THAT THE I-TH ENTRY OF THE PERMUTATION VECTOR   
5765     !C     P INDICATES THE ROW THE I-TH ROW GETS MAPPED INTO.  (I.E.     
5766     !C     IF ( P(I) = J ) ROW I GETS MAPPED INTO ROW J.)      
5767     !C       
5768     !C ... THE ARRAY NEWIA IS AN INTEGER WORK VECTOR OF LENGTH N WHICH   
5769     !C     KEEPS TRACK OF WHERE THE ROWS BEGIN IN THE PERMUTED STRUCTURE.
5770     !C       
5771     !C ... PERMAT IS CAPABLE OF PERMUTING BOTH THE SYMMETRIC AND NON-    
5772     !C     SYMMETRIC FORM OF IA, JA, AND A.  IF ( ISYM .EQ. 0 ) SYMMETRIC
5773     !C     FORM IS ASSUMED.      
5774     !C       
5775     !C ... TWO EXTERNAL MODULES ARE USED BY PERMAT.  THE FIRST IS INTEGER
5776     !C     FUNCTION BISRCH WHICH USES A BISECTION SEARCH ( ORDER LOG-BASE-2
5777     !C     OF N+1 ) THROUGH THE ARRAY IA TO FIND THE ROW INDEX OF AN ARBI- 
5778     !C     TRARY ENTRY EXTRACTED FROM THE ARRAY JA. THE SECOND IS SUBROUTINE 
5779     !C     QSORT WHICH PERFORMS A QUICK SORT TO PLACE THE ENTRIES IN     
5780     !C     THE PERMUTED ROWS IN COLUMN ORDER.
5781     !C       
5782     !C*********************************************************************
5783     !C       
5784     !      INTEGER NN,IA(1),JA(1),P(NN),NEWIA(NN),ISYM,IERR    
5785     !      DOUBLE PRECISION A(1) 
5786     !C       
5787     !C ... INTERNAL VARIABLES    
5788     !C       
5789     !      INTEGER BISRCH,I,IBGN,IEND,IP,IPP,J,JAJ,JP,IER,K,N,NELS,NEXT,NPL1 
5790     !C       
5791     !      DOUBLE PRECISION SAVE,TEMP      
5792     !C       
5793     !C*********************************************************************
5794     !C       
5795     !C ... PREPROCESSING PHASE   
5796     !C       
5797     !C ...... DETERMINE THE NUMBER OF NONZEROES IN THE ROWS OF THE PERMUTED
5798     !C        MATRIX AND STORE THAT IN NEWIA.  THEN SWEEP THRU NEWIA TO MAKE 
5799     !C        NEWIA(I) POINT TO THE BEGINNING OF EACH ROW IN THE PERMUTED
5800     !C        DATA STRUCTURE.  ALSO NEGATE ALL THE ENTRIES IN JA TO INDICATE 
5801     !C        THAT THOSE ENTRIES HAVE NOT BEEN MOVED YET.      
5802     !C       
5803     !      N = NN      
5804     !      IER = 0     
5805     !      NPL1 = N+1  
5806     !      NELS = IA(NPL1)-1     
5807     !      DO 10 I = 1,N 
5808     !         NEWIA(I) = 0       
5809     !   10 CONTINUE    
5810     !      DO 30 I = 1,N 
5811     !         IP = P(I)
5812     !         IBGN = IA(I)       
5813     !         IEND = IA(I+1)-1   
5814     !         IF (IBGN.GT.IEND) GO TO 90   
5815     !         DO 20 J = IBGN,IEND
5816     !            IPP = IP
5817     !            JAJ = JA(J)     
5818     !            JP = P(JAJ)     
5819     !            IF (ISYM.EQ.0.AND.IP.GT.JP) IPP = JP
5820     !            NEWIA(IPP) = NEWIA(IPP)+1 
5821     !            JA(J) = -JAJ    
5822     !   20    CONTINUE 
5823     !   30 CONTINUE    
5824     !      IBGN = 1    
5825     !      DO 40 I = 1,N 
5826     !         K = IBGN+NEWIA(I)  
5827     !         NEWIA(I) = IBGN    
5828     !         IBGN = K 
5829     !   40 CONTINUE    
5830     !C       
5831     !C ...... PREPROCESSING NOW FINISHED.  
5832     !C       
5833     !C ...... NOW PERMUTE JA AND A.  THIS PERMUTATION WILL PERFORM THE   
5834     !C        FOLLOWING STEPS    
5835     !C       
5836     !C           1.  FIND THE FIRST ENTRY IN JA NOT PERMUTED WHICH IS    
5837     !C               INDICATED BY AN NEGATIVE VALUE IN JA      
5838     !C           2.  COMPUTE WHICH ROW THE CURRENT ENTRY IS IN.  THIS    
5839     !C               IS COMPUTED BY A BISECTION SEARCH THRU THE ARRAY    
5840     !C               IA. 
5841     !C           3.  USING THE PERMUTATION ARRAY P AND THE ARRAY NEWIA   
5842     !C               COMPUTE WHERE THE CURRENT ENTRY IS TO BE PLACED.    
5843     !C           4.  THEN PICK UP THE ENTRY WHERE THE CURRENT ENTRY WILL 
5844     !C               GO.  PUT THE CURRENT ENTRY IN PLACE.  THEN MAKE THE 
5845     !C               DISPLACED ENTRY THE CURRENT ENTRY AND LOOP TO STEP 2. 
5846     !C           5.  THIS PROCESS WILL END WHEN THE NEXT ENTRY HAS ALREADY 
5847     !C               BEEN MOVED.  THEN LOOP TO STEP 1. 
5848     !C       
5849     !      DO 70 J = 1,NELS      
5850     !         IF (JA(J).GT.0) GO TO 70     
5851     !         JAJ = -JA(J)       
5852     !         SAVE = A(J)
5853     !         NEXT = J 
5854     !         JA(J) = JAJ
5855     !C       
5856     !   50    JP = P(JAJ)
5857     !         I = BISRCH(NPL1,IA,NEXT)     
5858     !         IP = P(I)
5859     !         IPP = IP 
5860     !         IF (ISYM.NE.0.OR.IP.LE.JP) GO TO 60    
5861     !         IPP = JP 
5862     !         JP = IP  
5863     !   60    NEXT = NEWIA(IPP)  
5864     !C       
5865     !         TEMP = SAVE
5866     !         SAVE = A(NEXT)     
5867     !         A(NEXT) = TEMP     
5868     !C       
5869     !         JAJ = -JA(NEXT)    
5870     !         JA(NEXT) = JP      
5871     !         NEWIA(IPP) = NEWIA(IPP)+1    
5872     !         IF (JAJ.GT.0) GO TO 50       
5873     !C       
5874     !   70 CONTINUE    
5875     !C       
5876     !C ...... THE MATRIX IS NOW PERMUTED BUT THE ROWS MAY NOT BE IN      
5877     !C        ORDER.  THE REMAINDER OF THIS SUBROUTINE PERFORMS
5878     !C        A QUICK SORT ON EACH ROW TO SORT THE ENTRIES IN  
5879     !C        COLUMN ORDER.  THE IA ARRAY IS ALSO CORRECTED FROM 
5880     !C        INFORMATION STORED IN THE NEWIA ARRAY.  NEWIA(I) NOW       
5881     !C        POINTS TO THE FIRST ENTRY OF ROW I+1.  
5882     !C       
5883     !      IA(1) = 1   
5884     !      DO 80 I = 1,N 
5885     !         IA(I+1) = NEWIA(I) 
5886     !         K = IA(I+1)-IA(I)  
5887     !         IF (K.EQ.1) GO TO 80 
5888     !         IF (K.LT.1) GO TO 110
5889     !C       
5890     !         IBGN = IA(I)       
5891     !         CALL QSORT (K,JA(IBGN),A(IBGN),IER)    
5892     !         IF (IER.NE.0) GO TO 130      
5893     !C       
5894     !   80 CONTINUE    
5895     !C       
5896     !C ...... END OF MATRIX PERMUTATION    
5897     !C       
5898     !      GO TO 150   
5899     !C       
5900     !C ... ERROR TRAPS 
5901     !C       
5902     !C ...... NO ENTRY IN ROW I IN THE ORIGINAL SYSTEM 
5903     !C       
5904     !   90 IER = 301   
5905     !      IF (LEVEL.GE.0) WRITE (NOUT,100) I
5906     !  100 FORMAT ('0','*** F A T A L     E R R O R ************'/'0',   
5907     !     *   '    IN ITPACK ROUTINE PERMAT  '/' ','    NO ENTRY IN ROW ',I10
5908     !     *   ,' OF ORIGINAL MATRIX ')     
5909     !      GO TO 150   
5910     !C       
5911     !C ...... NO ENTRY IN ROW I IN THE PERMUTED SYSTEM 
5912     !C       
5913     !  110 IER = 302   
5914     !      IF (LEVEL.GE.0) WRITE (NOUT,120) I
5915     !  120 FORMAT ('0','*** F A T A L     E R R O R ************'/'0',   
5916     !     *   '    IN ITPACK ROUTINE PRBNDX  '/' ','    NO ENTRY IN ROW ',I10
5917     !     *   ,' OF PERMUTED MATRIX ')     
5918     !      GO TO 150   
5919     !C       
5920     !C ...... ERROR RETURN FROM SUBROUTINE QSORT     
5921     !C       
5922     !  130 IER = 303   
5923     !      IF (LEVEL.GE.0) WRITE (NOUT,140) I
5924     !  140 FORMAT ('0','*** F A T A L     E R R O R ************'/'0',   
5925     !     *   '    IN ITPACK ROUTINE QSORT   '/' ',  
5926     !     *   '    ERROR IN SORTING PERMUTED ROW ',I12/' ',    
5927     !     *   '    CALLED FROM ITPACK ROUTINE PRBNDX   ')      
5928     !C       
5929     !  150 CONTINUE    
5930     !      IERR = IER  
5931     !      RETURN      
5932     !      END 
5933     !      SUBROUTINE PERROR (NN,IA,JA,A,RHS,U,W,DIGTT1,DIGTT2,IDGTTS)   
5934     !C       
5935     !C     PERROR COMPUTES THE RESIDUAL, R = RHS - A*U.  THE USER
5936     !C     ALSO HAS THE OPTION OF PRINTING THE RESIDUAL AND/OR THE       
5937     !C     UNKNOWN VECTOR DEPENDING ON IDGTS.
5938     !C       
5939     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
5940     !C       
5941     !C          N      DIMENSION OF MATRIX (= NN)    
5942     !C          IA,JA  INTEGER ARRAYS OF SPARSE MATRIX REPRESENTATION    
5943     !C          A      D.P. ARRAY OF SPARSE MATRIX REPRESENTATION
5944     !C          RHS    RIGHT HAND SIDE OF MATRIX PROBLEM       
5945     !C          U      LATEST ESTIMATE OF SOLUTION   
5946     !C          W      WORKSPACE VECTOR    
5947     !C          DIGIT1 OUTPUT: MEASURE OF ACCURACY OF STOPPING TEST (= DIGTT1
5948     !C          DIGIT2 OUTPUT: MEASURE OF ACCURACY OF SOLUTION (= DIGTT2)
5949     !C          IDGTS   PARAMETER CONTROLING LEVEL OF OUTPUT (= IDGTTS)  
5950     !C                    IF IDGTS < 1 OR IDGTS > 4, THEN NO OUTPUT.     
5951     !C                            = 1, THEN NUMBER OF DIGITS IS PRINTED, PRO-
5952     !C                                 VIDED LEVEL .GE. 1      
5953     !C                            = 2, THEN SOLUTION VECTOR IS PRINTED, PRO- 
5954     !C                                 VIDED LEVEL .GE. 1      
5955     !C                            = 3, THEN RESIDUAL VECTOR IS PRINTED, PRO- 
5956     !C                                 VIDED LEVEL .GE. 1      
5957     !C                            = 4, THEN BOTH VECTORS ARE PRINTED, PRO- 
5958     !C                                 VIDED LEVEL .GE. 1      
5959     !C       
5960     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR ARGUMENTS    
5961     !C       
5962     !      INTEGER IA(1),JA(1),NN,IDGTTS   
5963     !      DOUBLE PRECISION A(1),RHS(NN),U(NN),W(NN),DIGTT1,DIGTT2       
5964     !C       
5965     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR LOCAL VARIABLES
5966     !C       
5967     !      INTEGER IDGTS,N       
5968     !      DOUBLE PRECISION BNRM,DIGIT1,DIGIT2,RNRM,TEMP       
5969     !C       
5970     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR FUNCTION SUBPROGRAMS   
5971     !C       
5972     !      DOUBLE PRECISION DDOT 
5973     !C       
5974     !C *** BEGIN: ITPACK COMMON  
5975     !C       
5976     !      INTEGER IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT       
5977     !      COMMON /ITCOM1/ IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT 
5978     !C       
5979     !      LOGICAL ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD   
5980     !      COMMON /ITCOM2/ ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD     
5981     !C       
5982     !      DOUBLE PRECISION BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA,
5983     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
5984     !      COMMON /ITCOM3/ BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA, 
5985     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
5986     !C       
5987     !C *** END  : ITPACK COMMON  
5988     !C       
5989     !C     DESCRIPTION OF VARIABLES IN COMMON BLOCK IN MAIN SUBROUTINE   
5990     !C       
5991     !      N = NN      
5992     !      IDGTS = IDGTTS
5993     !      DIGIT1 = 0.D0 
5994     !      DIGIT2 = 0.D0 
5995     !      IF (N.LE.0) GO TO 40  
5996     !C       
5997     !      DIGIT1 = -DLOG10(DABS(DRELPR))  
5998     !      IF (STPTST.GT.0.D0) DIGIT1 = -DLOG10(DABS(STPTST))  
5999     !      BNRM = DDOT(N,RHS,1,RHS,1)      
6000     !      IF (BNRM.EQ.0.D0) GO TO 10      
6001     !      CALL PMULT (N,IA,JA,A,U,W)      
6002     !      CALL WEVMW (N,RHS,W)  
6003     !      RNRM = DDOT(N,W,1,W,1)
6004     !      TEMP = RNRM/BNRM      
6005     !      IF (TEMP.EQ.0.D0) GO TO 10      
6006     !      DIGIT2 = -DLOG10(DABS(TEMP))/2.D0 
6007     !      GO TO 20    
6008     !C       
6009     !   10 DIGIT2 = -DLOG10(DABS(DRELPR))  
6010     !C       
6011     !   20 IF ((IDGTS.LT.1).OR.(LEVEL.LE.0)) GO TO 40
6012     !      WRITE (NOUT,30) DIGIT1,DIGIT2   
6013     !   30 FORMAT (/6X,'APPROX. NO. OF DIGITS (EST. REL. ERROR) =',F5.1,2X,
6014     !     *   '(DIGIT1)'/3X,'APPROX. NO. OF DIGITS (EST. REL. RESIDUAL) =',
6015     !     *   F5.1,2X,'(DIGIT2)')
6016     !C       
6017     !      IF (IDGTS.LE.1.OR.IDGTS.GT.4) GO TO 40    
6018     !      IF (IDGTS.NE.3) CALL VOUT (N,U,2,NOUT)    
6019     !      IF (IDGTS.GE.3) CALL VOUT (N,W,1,NOUT)    
6020     !C       
6021     !   40 CONTINUE    
6022     !      DIGTT1 = DIGIT1       
6023     !      DIGTT2 = DIGIT2       
6024     !      RETURN      
6025     !      END

6390     !            JAJJ = JA(JJ)   
6391     !            WII = WII+A(JJ)*U(JAJJ)   
6392     !            W(JAJJ) = W(JAJJ)+A(JJ)*UII 
6393     !   50    CONTINUE 
6394     !   60    W(II) = WII
6395     !   70 CONTINUE    
6396     !      RETURN      
6397     !C       
6398     !      END 
6399     !      SUBROUTINE PRBNDX (NN,NBLACK,IA,JA,P,IP,LEVEL,NOUT,IER)       
6400     !C       
6401     !C**************************************************************     
6402     !C       
6403     !C     THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTES THE RED-BLACK PERMUTATION  
6404     !C     VECTORS P ( AND ITS INVERSE IP ) IF POSSIBLE.       
6405     !C       
6406     !C     THE ALGORITHM IS TO MARK THE FIRST NODE AS RED (ARBITRARY).   
6407     !C     ALL OF ITS ADJACENT NODES ARE MARKED BLACK AND PLACED IN      
6408     !C     A STACK.  THE REMAINDER OF THE CODE PULLS THE FIRST NODE      
6409     !C     OFF THE TOP OF THE STACK AND TRIES TO TYPE ITS ADJACENT NODES.
6410     !C     THE TYPING OF THE ADJACENT POINT IS A FIVE WAY CASE STATEMENT 
6411     !C     WHICH IS WELL COMMENTED BELOW (SEE DO LOOP 100).    
6412     !C       
6413     !C     THE ARRAY P IS USED BOTH TO KEEP TRACK OF THE COLOR OF A NODE 
6414     !C     (RED NODE IS POSITIVE, BLACK IS NEGATIVE) BUT ALSO THE FATHER 
6415     !C     NODE THAT CAUSED THE COLOR MARKING OF THAT POINT.  SINCE      
6416     !C     COMPLETE INFORMATION ON THE ADJACENCY STRUCTURE IS HARD TO COME 
6417     !C     BY THIS FORMS A LINK TO ENABLE THE COLOR CHANGE OF A PARTIAL  
6418     !C     TREE WHEN A RECOVERABLE COLOR CONFLICT OCCURS.      
6419     !C       
6420     !C     THE ARRAY IP IS USED AS A STACK TO POINT TO THE SET OF NODES  
6421     !C     LEFT TO BE TYPED THAT ARE KNOWN TO BE ADJACENT TO THE CURRENT 
6422     !C     FATHER NODE.
6423     !C       
6424     !C*********************************************************************
6425     !C       
6426     !C     INPUT PARAMETERS      
6427     !C       
6428     !C        N      NUMBER OF NODES.  (INTEGER, SCALAR) (= NN)
6429     !C       
6430     !C        IA,JA  ADJACENCY STRUCTURE ARRAYS.  CAN BE EITHER THE      
6431     !C               SYMMETRIC OR NONSYMMETRIC FORM.  IT IS ASSUMED      
6432     !C               THAT FOR EVERY ROW WHERE ONLY ONE ELEMENT IS
6433     !C               STORED THAT ELEMENT CORRESPONDS TO THE DIAGONAL     
6434     !C               ENTRY.  THE DIAGONAL DOES NOT HAVE TO BE THE FIRST  
6435     !C               ENTRY STORED.  (INTEGER, ARRAYS)
6436     !C        LEVEL  SWITCH FOR PRINTING   
6437     !C        NOUT OUTPUT TAPE NUMBER      
6438     !C       
6439     !C     OUTPUT PARAMETERS     
6440     !C       
6441     !C        NBLACK NUMBER OF BLACK NODES.  NUMBER OF RED NODES IS      
6442     !C               N - NBLACK.  (INTEGER, SCALAR)  
6443     !C       
6444     !C        P, IP  PERMUTATION AND INVERSE PERMUTATION VECTORS.
6445     !C               (INTEGER, ARRAYS EACH OF LENGTH N)
6446     !C       
6447     !C        IER    ERROR FLAG. (INTEGER, SCALAR)   
6448     !C       
6449     !C               IER = 0, NORMAL RETURN.  INDEXING PERFORMED 
6450     !C                        SUCCESSFULLY 
6451     !C               IER =201, RED-BLACK INDEXING NOT POSSIBLE.
6452     !C       
6453     !C******************************************************************** 
6454     !C       
6455     !      INTEGER NN,NBLACK,IA(1),JA(1),P(NN),IP(NN),IER      
6456     !C       
6457     !      INTEGER FIRST,NEXT,LAST,I,OLD,YOUNG,IBGN,IEND,J,K,CURTYP,NXTTYP,
6458     !     *   TYPE,NRED,N
6459     !C       
6460     !C-----------------------------------------------------------------------
6461     !C       
6462     !      N = NN      
6463     !      IER = 0     
6464     !C       
6465     !C        IF ( N .LE. 0 ) GO TO 8000   
6466     !C       
6467     !      DO 10 I = 1,N 
6468     !         P(I) = 0 
6469     !         IP(I) = 0
6470     !   10 CONTINUE    
6471     !C       
6472     !C ... HANDLE THE FIRST SET OF POINTS UNTIL SOME ADJACENT POINTS     
6473     !C ... ARE FOUND   
6474     !C       
6475     !      FIRST = 1   
6476     !C       
6477     !   20 P(FIRST) = FIRST      
6478     !      IF (IA(FIRST+1)-IA(FIRST).GT.1) GO TO 40  
6479     !C       
6480     !C ... SEARCH FOR NEXT ENTRY THAT HAS NOT BEEN MARKED      
6481     !C       
6482     !      IF (FIRST.EQ.N) GO TO 130       
6483     !      IBGN = FIRST+1
6484     !      DO 30 I = IBGN,N      
6485     !         IF (P(I).NE.0) GO TO 30      
6486     !         FIRST = I
6487     !         GO TO 20 
6488     !   30 CONTINUE    
6489     !      GO TO 130   
6490     !C       
6491     !C ... FIRST SET OF ADJACENT POINTS FOUND
6492     !C       
6493     !   40 NEXT = 1    
6494     !      LAST = 1    
6495     !      IP(1) = FIRST 
6496     !C       
6497     !C ... LOOP OVER LABELED POINTS INDICATED IN THE STACK STORED IN     
6498     !C ... THE ARRAY IP
6499     !C       
6500     !   50 K = IP(NEXT)
6501     !      CURTYP = P(K) 
6502     !      NXTTYP = -CURTYP      
6503     !      IBGN = IA(K)
6504     !      IEND = IA(K+1)-1      
6505     !      IF (IBGN.GT.IEND) GO TO 110     
6506     !      DO 100 I = IBGN,IEND  
6507     !         J = JA(I)
6508     !         TYPE = P(J)
6509     !         IF (J.EQ.K) GO TO 100
6510     !C       
6511     !C================================================================== 
6512     !C       
6513     !C     THE FOLLOWING IS A FIVE WAY CASE STATEMENT DEALING WITH THE   
6514     !C     LABELING OF THE ADJACENT NODE.  
6515     !C       
6516     !C ... CASE I.  IF THE ADJACENT NODE HAS ALREADY BEEN LABELED WITH   
6517     !C              LABEL EQUAL TO NXTTYP, THEN SKIP TO THE NEXT ADJACENT
6518     !C              NODE.
6519     !C       
6520     !         IF (TYPE.EQ.NXTTYP) GO TO 100
6521     !C       
6522     !C ... CASE II.  IF THE ADJACENT NODE HAS NOT BEEN LABELED YET LABEL 
6523     !C               IT WITH NXTTYP AND ENTER IT IN THE STACK  
6524     !C       
6525     !         IF (TYPE.NE.0) GO TO 60      
6526     !         LAST = LAST+1      
6527     !         IP(LAST) = J       
6528     !         P(J) = NXTTYP      
6529     !         GO TO 100
6530     !C       
6531     !C ... CASE III.  IF THE ADJACENT NODE HAS ALREADY BEEN LABELED WITH 
6532     !C                OPPOSITE COLOR AND THE SAME FATHER SEED, THEN THERE
6533     !C                IS AN IRRECOVERABLE COLOR CONFLICT.      
6534     !C       
6535     !   60    IF (TYPE.EQ.CURTYP) GO TO 160
6536     !C       
6537     !C ... CASE IV.  IF THE ADJACENT NODE HAS THE RIGHT COLOR AND A DIFFERENT
6538     !C               FATHER NODE, THEN CHANGE ALL NODES OF THE YOUNGEST FATHE
6539     !C               NODE TO POINT TO THE OLDEST FATHER SEED AND RETAIN THE
6540     !C               SAME COLORS.
6541     !C       
6542     !         IF (TYPE*NXTTYP.LT.1) GO TO 80 
6543     !         OLD = MIN0(IABS(TYPE),IABS(NXTTYP))    
6544     !         YOUNG = MAX0(IABS(TYPE),IABS(NXTTYP))  
6545     !         DO 70 J = YOUNG,N  
6546     !            IF (IABS(P(J)).EQ.YOUNG) P(J) = ISIGN(OLD,P(J)) 
6547     !   70    CONTINUE 
6548     !         CURTYP = P(K)      
6549     !         NXTTYP = -CURTYP   
6550     !         GO TO 100
6551     !C       
6552     !C ... CASE V.  IF THE ADJACENT NODE HAS THE WRONG COLOR AND A DIFFERENT 
6553     !C              FATHER NODE, THEN CHANGE ALL NODES OF THE YOUNGEST FATHER
6554     !C              NODE TO POINT TO THE OLDEST FATHER NODE ALONG WITH   
6555     !C              CHANGING THEIR COLORS.  SINCE UNTIL THIS TIME THE    
6556     !C              YOUNGEST FATHER NODE TREE HAS BEEN INDEPENDENT NO OTHER
6557     !C              COLOR CONFLICTS WILL ARISE FROM THIS CHANGE. 
6558     !C       
6559     !   80    OLD = MIN0(IABS(TYPE),IABS(NXTTYP))    
6560     !         YOUNG = MAX0(IABS(TYPE),IABS(NXTTYP))  
6561     !         DO 90 J = YOUNG,N  
6562     !            IF (IABS(P(J)).EQ.YOUNG) P(J) = ISIGN(OLD,-P(J))
6563     !   90    CONTINUE 
6564     !         CURTYP = P(K)      
6565     !         NXTTYP = -CURTYP   
6566     !C       
6567     !C ... END OF CASE STATEMENT 
6568     !C       
6569     !C================================================================== 
6570     !C       
6571     !  100 CONTINUE    
6572     !C       
6573     !C ... ADVANCE TO NEXT NODE IN THE STACK 
6574     !C       
6575     !  110 NEXT = NEXT+1 
6576     !      IF (NEXT.LE.LAST) GO TO 50      
6577     !C       
6578     !C ... ALL NODES IN THE STACK HAVE BEEN REMOVED  
6579     !C       
6580     !C ... CHECK FOR NODES NOT LABELED.  IF ANY ARE FOUND      
6581     !C ... START THE LABELING PROCESS AGAIN AT THE FIRST       
6582     !C ... NODE FOUND THAT IS NOT LABELED. 
6583     !C       
6584     !      IBGN = FIRST+1
6585     !      DO 120 I = IBGN,N     
6586     !         IF (P(I).NE.0) GO TO 120     
6587     !         FIRST = I
6588     !         GO TO 20 
6589     !  120 CONTINUE    
6590     !C       
6591     !C===================================================================
6592     !C       
6593     !C ... ALL NODES ARE NOW TYPED EITHER RED OR BLACK 
6594     !C       
6595     !C ... GENERATE PERMUTATION VECTORS    
6596     !C       
6597     !  130 NRED = 0    
6598     !      NBLACK = 0  
6599     !      DO 150 I = 1,N
6600     !         IF (P(I).LT.0) GO TO 140     
6601     !C       
6602     !C       RED POINT 
6603     !C       
6604     !         NRED = NRED+1      
6605     !         IP(NRED) = I       
6606     !         P(I) = NRED
6607     !         GO TO 150
6608     !C       
6609     !C     BLACK POINT 
6610     !C       
6611     !  140    NBLACK = NBLACK+1  
6612     !         J = N-NBLACK+1     
6613     !         IP(J) = I
6614     !         P(I) = J 
6615     !C       
6616     !  150 CONTINUE    
6617     !C       
6618     !C ... SUCCESSFUL RED-BLACK ORDERING COMPLETED   
6619     !C       
6620     !      GO TO 180   
6621     !C       
6622     !C ........ ERROR TRAPS      
6623     !C       
6624     !C ...... N .LE. 0 
6625     !C       
6626     !C8000    IER = 200
6627     !C        GO TO 9000 
6628     !C       
6629     !C ...... TYPE CONFLICT      
6630     !C       
6631     !  160 IER = 201   
6632     !      IF (LEVEL.GE.0) WRITE (NOUT,170)
6633     !  170 FORMAT ('0','*** F A T A L     E R R O R ************'/'0',   
6634     !     *   '    IN ITPACK ROUTINE PRBNDX  '/' ',  
6635     !     *   '    RED-BLACK INDEXING NOT POSSIBLE') 
6636     !C       
6637     !C ... RETURN      
6638     !C       
6639     !  180 CONTINUE    
6640     !      RETURN      
6641     !      END 
6642     !      SUBROUTINE PRSBLK (NNB,NNR,IA,JA,A,UR,VB) 
6643     !C

6645     !C       
6646     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
6647     !C

6649     !C         NR      NUMBER OF RED POINTS (= NNR)

6654     !C                    VECTOR

6678     !C       
6679     !C *** END  : ITPACK COMMON  
6680     !C       
6681     !C     DESCRIPTION OF VARIABLES IN COMMON BLOCK IN MAIN SUBROUTINE   
6682     !C       
6683     !      NB = NNB    
6684     !      NR = NNR    
6685     !      IF (ISYM.EQ.0) GO TO 30 
6686     !C

6690     !         INR = I+NR

6757     !      SUBROUTINE PSSOR1 (NN,IA,JA,A,U,RHS,FR,BR)
6758     !C       
6759     !C     ... COMPUTES COMPLETE SSOR SWEEP ON U.  U IS OVERWRITTEN      
6760     !C     ... WITH THE NEW ITERANT, FR AND BR WILL CONTAIN    
6761     !C     ... THE FORWARD AND BACKWARD RESIDUALS ON OUTPUT.   
6762     !C       
6763     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
6764     !C       
6765     !C         N       ORDER OF SYSTEM (= NN)
6766     !C          OMEGA  RELAXATION FACTOR   
6767     !C          IA,JA  INTEGER ARRAYS OF SPARSE MATRIX REPRESENTATION    
6768     !C          A      D.P. ARRAY OF SPARSE MATRIX REPRESENTATION
6769     !C          U      ESTIMATE OF SOLUTION
6770     !C          RHS    RIGHT HAND SIDE OF MATRIX PROBLEM       
6771     !C          FR,BR  OUTPUT: FORWARD AND BACKWARD RESIDUALS RESPECTIVELY 
6772     !C       
6773     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR ARGUMENTS    
6774     !C       
6775     !      INTEGER IA(1),JA(1),NN
6776     !      DOUBLE PRECISION A(1),U(NN),RHS(NN),FR(NN),BR(NN)   
6777     !C       
6778     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR LOCAL VARIABLES
6779     !C       
6780     !      INTEGER I,IBGN,IEND,II,JAJJ,JJ,N,NPL1     
6781     !      DOUBLE PRECISION OMM1,SUM,UII   
6782     !C       
6783     !C *** BEGIN: ITPACK COMMON  
6784     !C       
6785     !      INTEGER IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT       
6786     !      COMMON /ITCOM1/ IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT 
6787     !C       
6788     !      LOGICAL ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD   
6789     !      COMMON /ITCOM2/ ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD     
6790     !C       
6791     !      DOUBLE PRECISION BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA,
6792     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
6793     !      COMMON /ITCOM3/ BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA, 
6794     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
6795     !C       
6796     !C *** END  : ITPACK COMMON  
6797     !C       
6798     !C     DESCRIPTION OF VARIABLES IN COMMON BLOCK IN MAIN SUBROUTINE   
6799     !C       
6800     !      N = NN      
6801     !      NPL1 = N+1  
6802     !      OMM1 = OMEGA-1.D0     
6803     !      IF (ISYM.EQ.0) GO TO 40 
6804     !C       
6805     !C     *************** NON - SYMMETRIC SECTION **********************
6806     !C       
6807     !C     ... FORWARD SWEEP     
6808     !C       
6809     !      DO 30 II = 1,N
6810     !         BR(II) = U(II)     
6811     !         IBGN = IA(II)      
6812     !         IEND = IA(II+1)-1  
6813     !         SUM = RHS(II)      
6814     !         IF (IBGN.GT.IEND) GO TO 20   
6815     !         DO 10 JJ = IBGN,IEND 
6816     !            JAJJ = JA(JJ)   
6817     !            SUM = SUM-A(JJ)*U(JAJJ)   
6818     !   10    CONTINUE 
6819     !   20    UII = OMEGA*SUM-OMM1*U(II)   
6820     !         FR(II) = UII-U(II) 
6821     !         U(II) = UII
6822     !   30 CONTINUE    
6823     !      GO TO 90    
6824     !C       
6825     !C     ***************** SYMMETRIC SECTION **************************
6826     !C       
6827     !C     ... FORWARD SWEEP     
6828     !C       
6829     !   40 DO 80 II = 1,N
6830     !         BR(II) = U(II)     
6831     !         IBGN = IA(II)      
6832     !         IEND = IA(II+1)-1  
6833     !         SUM = RHS(II)      
6834     !         IF (IBGN.GT.IEND) GO TO 60   
6835     !         DO 50 JJ = IBGN,IEND 
6836     !            JAJJ = JA(JJ)   
6837     !            SUM = SUM-A(JJ)*U(JAJJ)   
6838     !   50    CONTINUE 
6839     !   60    UII = OMEGA*SUM-OMM1*U(II)   
6840     !         FR(II) = UII-U(II) 
6841     !         U(II) = UII
6842     !         IF (IBGN.GT.IEND) GO TO 80   
6843     !         DO 70 JJ = IBGN,IEND 
6844     !            JAJJ = JA(JJ)   
6845     !            RHS(JAJJ) = RHS(JAJJ)-A(JJ)*UII     
6846     !   70    CONTINUE 
6847     !   80 CONTINUE    
6848     !C       
6849     !C     ... BACKWARD SWEEP    
6850     !C       
6851     !   90 DO 120 I = 1,N
6852     !         II = NPL1-I
6853     !         IBGN = IA(II)      
6854     !         IEND = IA(II+1)-1  
6855     !         UII = RHS(II)      
6856     !         IF (IBGN.GT.IEND) GO TO 110  
6857     !         DO 100 JJ = IBGN,IEND
6858     !            JAJJ = JA(JJ)   
6859     !            UII = UII-A(JJ)*U(JAJJ)   
6860     !  100    CONTINUE 
6861     !  110    U(II) = OMEGA*UII-OMM1*U(II) 
6862     !         BR(II) = U(II)-BR(II)
6863     !  120 CONTINUE    
6864     !C       
6865     !      RETURN      
6866     !C       
6867     !      END 
6868     !      SUBROUTINE PSTOP (N,U,DNRM,CCON,IFLAG,Q1) 
6869     !C       
6870     !C     THIS SUBROUTINE PERFORMS A TEST TO SEE IF THE ITERATIVE       
6871     !C     METHOD HAS CONVERGED TO A SOLUTION INSIDE THE ERROR 
6872     !C     TOLERANCE, ZETA.      
6873     !C       
6874     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
6875     !C       
6876     !C          N      ORDER OF SYSTEM     
6877     !C          U      PRESENT SOLUTION ESTIMATE     
6878     !C          DNRM   INNER PRODUCT OF PSEUDO-RESIDUALS AT PRECEDING    
6879     !C                    ITERATION
6880     !C          CON    STOPPING TEST PARAMETER (= CCON)

6956     !      DOUBLE PRECISION FUNCTION PVTBV (N,IA,JA,A,V)       
6957     !C

7013     !      SUBROUTINE QSORT (NN,KEY,DATA,ERROR)      
7014     !C       
7015     !C     ==================================================================
7016     !C       
7017     !C     Q U I C K S O R T     
7018     !C       
7019     !C         IN THE STYLE OF THE CACM PAPER BY BOB SEDGEWICK, OCTOBER 1978 
7020     !C       
7021     !C     INPUT:      
7022     !C         N    -- NUMBER OF ELEMENTS TO BE SORTED (= NN)  
7023     !C         KEY  -- AN ARRAY OF LENGTH  N  CONTAINING THE VALUES      
7024     !C                 WHICH ARE TO BE SORTED
7025     !C         DATA -- A SECOND ARRAY OF LENGTH  N  CONTAINING DATA      
7026     !C                 ASSOCIATED WITH THE INDIVIDUAL KEYS.    
7027     !C       
7028     !C     OUTPUT:     
7029     !C         KEY  -- WILL BE ARRANGED SO THAT VALUES ARE IN INCREASING 
7030     !C                 ORDER     
7031     !C         DATA -- REARRANGED TO CORRESPOND TO REARRANGED KEYS       
7032     !C         ERROR -- WILL BE ZERO UNLESS YOUR INPUT FILE WAS OF TRULY 
7033     !C                  ENORMOUS LENGTH, IN WHICH CASE IT WILL BE EQUAL TO 1.
7034     !C       
7035     !C     ==================================================================

7037     !      INTEGER NN,ERROR,KEY(NN)
7038     !      DOUBLE PRECISION DATA(NN)       
7039     !C       
7040     !C     ------------------------
7041     !C       
7042     !      INTEGER TOP,LEFT,RIGHT,I,J,TINY,V,K,IP1,JM1,LLEN,RLEN,N       
7043     !      LOGICAL DONE
7044     !      DOUBLE PRECISION D    
7045     !      INTEGER STKLEN,STACK(30)
7046     !C       
7047     !      DATA TINY,STKLEN / 9,30 /       
7048     !C       
7049     !C     -----------------------------------       
7050     !C       
7051     !C     ... PROGRAM IS A DIRECT TRANSLATION INTO FORTRAN OF SEDGEWICK^S 
7052     !C         PROGRAM 2, WHICH IS NON-RECURSIVE, IGNORES FILES OF LENGTH
7053     !C         LESS THAN 'TINY' DURING PARTITIONING, AND USES MEDIAN OF THREE
7054     !C         PARTITIONING.     
7055     !C

7057     !      IF (N.EQ.1) RETURN    
7058     !      IF (N.LE.0) GO TO 240 
7059     !C       
7060     !      ERROR = 0   
7061     !      TOP = 1     
7062     !      LEFT = 1    
7063     !      RIGHT = N   
7064     !      DONE = (N.LE.TINY)    
7065     !C       
7066     !      IF (DONE) GO TO 150   
7067     !      CALL IVFILL (STKLEN,STACK,0)    
7068     !C       
7069     !C     ===========================================================   
7070     !C     QUICKSORT -- PARTITION THE FILE UNTIL NO SUBFILE REMAINS OF   
7071     !C     LENGTH GREATER THAN 'TINY'      
7072     !C     ===========================================================   
7073     !C       
7074     !C     ... WHILE NOT DONE DO ...       
7075     !C       
7076     !   10 IF (DONE) GO TO 150   
7077     !C       
7078     !C         ... FIND MEDIAN OF LEFT, RIGHT AND MIDDLE ELEMENTS OF CURRENT 
7079     !C             SUBFILE, WHICH IS  KEY(LEFT), ..., KEY(RIGHT) 
7080     !C       
7081     !      LFRH2 = (LEFT+RIGHT)/2
7082     !      K = KEY(LFRH2)
7083     !      D = DATA(LFRH2)

7085     !      DATA(LFRH2) = DATA(LEFT)
7086     !      KEY(LEFT) = K 
7087     !      DATA(LEFT) = D

7089     !      IF (KEY(LEFT+1).LE.KEY(RIGHT)) GO TO 20   
7090     !      K = KEY(LEFT+1)

7092     !      KEY(LEFT+1) = KEY(RIGHT)
7093     !      DATA(LEFT+1) = DATA(RIGHT)      
7094     !      KEY(RIGHT) = K
7095     !      DATA(RIGHT) = D       
7096     !C       
7097     !   20 IF (KEY(LEFT).LE.KEY(RIGHT)) GO TO 30     
7098     !      K = KEY(LEFT) 
7099     !      D = DATA(LEFT)
7100     !      KEY(LEFT) = KEY(RIGHT)
7101     !      DATA(LEFT) = DATA(RIGHT)
7102     !      KEY(RIGHT) = K
7103     !      DATA(RIGHT) = D       
7104     !C       
7105     !   30 IF (KEY(LEFT+1).LE.KEY(LEFT)) GO TO 40    
7106     !      K = KEY(LEFT+1)       
7107     !      D = DATA(LEFT+1)      
7108     !      KEY(LEFT+1) = KEY(LEFT) 
7109     !      DATA(LEFT+1) = DATA(LEFT)       
7110     !      KEY(LEFT) = K 
7111     !      DATA(LEFT) = D
7112     !C       
7113     !   40 V = KEY(LEFT) 
7114     !C       
7115     !C         ... V IS NOW THE MEDIAN VALUE OF THE THREE KEYS.  NOW MOVE
7116     !C             FROM THE LEFT AND RIGHT ENDS SIMULTANEOUSLY, EXCHANGING 
7117     !C             KEYS AND DATA UNTIL ALL KEYS LESS THAN  V  ARE PACKED TO
7118     !C             THE LEFT, ALL KEYS LARGER THAN  V  ARE PACKED TO THE  
7119     !C             RIGHT.

7122     !      J = RIGHT

7126     !C             REPEAT J = J-1 UNTIL KEY(J) <= V; 
7127     !C         EXIT IF J < I;

7129     !C         END     
7130     !C       
7131     !   50 CONTINUE    
7132     !   60 I = I+1     
7133     !      IF (KEY(I).LT.V) GO TO 60       
7134     !C       
7135     !   70 J = J-1     
7136     !      IF (KEY(J).GT.V) GO TO 70

7138     !      IF (J.LT.I) GO TO 80  
7139     !      K = KEY(I)  
7140     !      D = DATA(I) 
7141     !      KEY(I) = KEY(J)       
7142     !      DATA(I) = DATA(J)     
7143     !      KEY(J) = K  
7144     !      DATA(J) = D 
7145     !      GO TO 50    
7146     !C       
7147     !   80 K = KEY(LEFT) 
7148     !      D = DATA(LEFT)
7149     !      KEY(LEFT) = KEY(J)    
7150     !      DATA(LEFT) = DATA(J)

7152     !      DATA(J) = D

7155     !C             ONE IS (LEFT ... J-1)  AND THE OTHER IS (I...RIGHT).  
7156     !C             PROCESS THE SMALLER NEXT.  STACK THE LARGER ONE.      
7157     !C

7159     !      RLEN = RIGHT-I+1

7165     !      TOP = TOP-2

7169     !C       
7170     !   90 DONE = .TRUE. 
7171     !C

7173     !C

7175     !C       
7176     !  100 IF (MIN0(LLEN,RLEN).GT.TINY) GO TO 120    
7177     !C       
7178     !C             ... ONE SUBFILE IS SMALL, ONE LARGE.  IGNORE THE SMALL ONE
7179     !C       
7180     !      IF (LLEN.GT.RLEN) GO TO 110     
7181     !      LEFT = I    
7182     !      GO TO 10    
7183     !C       
7184     !  110 RIGHT = J-1 
7185     !C       
7186     !      GO TO 10    
7187     !C       
7188     !C         ... ELSE BOTH ARE LARGER THAN TINY.  ONE MUST BE STACKED. 
7189     !C

7191     !      IF (LLEN.GT.RLEN) GO TO 130     
7192     !      STACK(TOP) = I

7194     !      RIGHT = J-1 
7195     !      GO TO 140   
7196     !C

7198     !      STACK(TOP+1) = J-1    
7199     !      LEFT = I    
7200     !C       
7201     !  140 TOP = TOP+2 
7202     !C       
7203     !      GO TO 10    
7204     !C       
7205     !C     ------------------------------------------------------------  
7206     !C     INSERTION SORT THE ENTIRE FILE, WHICH CONSISTS OF A LIST      
7207     !C     OF 'TINY' SUBFILES, LOCALLY OUT OF ORDER, GLOBALLY IN ORDER.  
7208     !C     ------------------------------------------------------------  
7209     !C       
7210     !C     ... FIRST, FIND LARGEST ELEMENT IN 'KEY'  
7211     !C       
7212     !  150 I = N-1     
7213     !      LEFT = MAX0(0,N-TINY)

7218     !      IF (KEY(I).LE.K) GO TO 170

7270     !      SUBROUTINE SBAGN (N,NZ,IA,JA,A,IWORK,LEVELL,NOUTT,IERR)       
7271     !C       
7272     !C ... THE ROUTINES SBINI, SBSIJ, AND SBEND CREATE A SPARSE
7273     !C     MATRIX STRUCTURE BY MEANS OF A LINKED LIST WHICH IS 
7274     !C     DESTROYED BY SBEND. SBAGN CREATES A NEW LINKED LIST 
7275     !C     SO THAT ELEMENTS MAY BE ADDED TO THE MATRIX AFTER SBEND       
7276     !C     HAS BEEN CALLED. SBAGN SHOULD BE CALLED WITH THE APPRO-       
7277     !C     PRIATE PARAMETERS, AND THEN SBSIJ AND SBEND CAN BE CALLED     
7278     !C     TO ADD THE ELEMENTS AND COMPLETE THE SPARSE MATRIX STRUC-     
7279     !C     TURE.       
7280     !C       
7281     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
7282     !C       
7283     !C           N       ORDER OF THE SYSTEM 
7284     !C           NZ      MAXIMUM NUMBER OF NON-ZERO ELEMENTS   
7285     !C                   IN THE SYSTEM     
7286     !C           IA, JA  INTEGER ARRAYS OF THE SPARSE
7287     !C                   MATRIX STRUCTURE  
7288     !C           A       D.P. ARRAY OF THE SPARSE MATRIX       
7289     !C                   STRUCTURE 
7290     !C           IWORK   WORK ARRAY OF DIMENSION NZ  
7291     !C           LEVEL   OUTPUT LEVEL CONTROL (= LEVELL)       
7292     !C           NOUT  OUTPUT FILE NUMBER (= NOUTT)  
7293     !C           IER     ERROR FLAG (= IERR). POSSIBLE RETURNS ARE       
7294     !C                      IER = 0, SUCCESSFUL COMPLETION     
7295     !C                          = 703, NZ TOO SMALL - NO MORE  
7296     !C                                 ELEMENTS CAN BE ADDED   
7297     !C       
7298     !C ... SPECIFICTIONS FOR ARGUMENTS     
7299     !C       
7300     !      INTEGER NZ,IA(1),JA(1),IWORK(NZ),N,LEVELL,NOUTT,IERR
7301     !      DOUBLE PRECISION A(NZ)
7302     !C       
7303     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR LOCAL VARIABLES
7304     !C       
7305     !      INTEGER I,IER,J,LEVEL,NOUT,NADD,NADDP1,NOW,NP1,NTO,NTN
7306     !C       
7307     !C ... INITIALIZE LOCAL VARIABLES AND MAKE ERROR CHECK     
7308     !C       
7309     !      NOW = IA(N+1)-1       
7310     !      NADD = NZ-NOW 
7311     !      IER = 0     
7312     !      LEVEL = LEVELL
7313     !      NOUT = NOUTT
7314     !      IF (NADD.LE.0) IER = 703
7315     !      IF (IER.EQ.0) GO TO 20
7316     !      IF (LEVEL.GE.0) WRITE (NOUT,10) IER       
7317     !   10 FORMAT ('0','*** F A T A L     E R R O R ************'/'0',   
7318     !     *   '    IN ITPACK ROUTINE SBAGN   '/' ','    IER = ',I10/' ', 
7319     !     *   '    NZ TOO SMALL - NO ROOM FOR NEW ENTRY')      
7320     !      GO TO 90    
7321     !C       
7322     !C ... SHIFT ELEMENTS OF A AND JA DOWN AND ADD ZERO FILL   
7323     !C       
7324     !   20 NTO = NOW   
7325     !      NTN = NZ    
7326     !      DO 30 I = 1,NOW       
7327     !         JA(NTN) = JA(NTO)  
7328     !         A(NTN) = A(NTO)    
7329     !         NTO = NTO-1
7330     !         NTN = NTN-1
7331     !   30 CONTINUE    
7332     !      DO 40 I = 1,NADD      
7333     !         JA(I) = 0
7334     !         A(I) = 0.D0
7335     !   40 CONTINUE    
7336     !C       
7337     !C ... UPDATE IA TO REFLECT DOWNWARD SHIFT IN A AND JA     
7338     !C       
7339     !      NP1 = N+1   
7340     !      DO 50 I = 1,NP1       
7341     !         IA(I) = IA(I)+NADD 
7342     !   50 CONTINUE    
7343     !C       
7344     !C ... CREATE LINKED LIST    
7345     !C       
7346     !      NADDP1 = NADD+1       
7347     !      DO 60 I = NADDP1,NZ   
7348     !         IWORK(I) = I+1     
7349     !   60 CONTINUE    
7350     !      DO 70 I = 1,NADD      
7351     !         IWORK(I) = 0       
7352     !   70 CONTINUE    
7353     !      DO 80 I = 1,N 
7354     !         J = IA(I+1)-1      
7355     !         IWORK(J) = -I      
7356     !   80 CONTINUE    
7357     !C       
7358     !C ... INDICATE IN LAST POSITION OF IA HOW MANY SPACES     
7359     !C     ARE LEFT IN A AND JA FOR ADDITION OF ELEMENTS       
7360     !C       
7361     !      IA(N+1) = NADD
7362     !      RETURN      
7363     !C       
7364     !C ... ERROR RETURN
7365     !C       
7366     !   90 IERR = IER  
7367     !      RETURN      
7368     !      END 
7369     !      SUBROUTINE SBELM (NN,IA,JA,A,RHS,IW,RW,TOL,ISYM,LEVEL,NOUT,IER) 
7370     !C       
7371     !C ... SBELM IS DESIGNED TO REMOVE ROWS AND COLUMNS OF THE MATRIX    
7372     !C ... WHERE DABS(A(I,J))/A(I,I) .LE. TOL FOR J = 1 TO N AND A(I,I)  
7373     !C ... .GT. 0. THIS IS TO TAKE CARE OF MATRICES ARISING    
7374     !C ... FROM FINITE ELEMENT DISCRETIZATIONS OF PDE^S WITH DIRICHLET   
7375     !C ... BOUNDARY CONDITIONS.  ANY SUCH ROWS AND CORRESPONDING COLUMNS 
7376     !C ... ARE THEN SET TO THE IDENTITY AFTER CORRECTING RHS.  
7377     !C       
7378     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
7379     !C       
7380     !C          N      DIMENSION OF MATRIX (= NN)    
7381     !C          IA,JA  INTEGER ARRAYS OF SPARSE MATRIX REPRESENTATION    
7382     !C          A      D.P. ARRAY OF SPARSE MATRIX REPRESENTATION
7383     !C          RHS    RIGHT HAND SIDE OF MATRIX PROBLEM       
7384     !C          IW,RW  WORK ARRAYS OF LENGTH N       
7385     !C          TOL    TOLERANCE FACTOR    
7386     !C          ISYM   FLAG FOR TYPE OF STORAGE FOR SYSTEM     
7387     !C                 (0: SYMMETRIC, 1:NONSYMMETRIC)
7388     !C          LEVEL  PRINTING SWITCH FOR ERROR CONDITION     
7389     !C          NOUT OUTPUT TAPE NUMBER    
7390     !C          IER    ERROR FLAG: NONZERO VALUE ON RETURN MEANS 
7391     !C                    101 : DIAGONAL ENTRY NOT POSITIVE    
7392     !C                    102 : THERE IS NO DIAGONAL ENTRY IN ROW
7393     !C       
7394     !C********************************************************************** 
7395     !C       
7396     !C     UPDATE.  SBELM HAS BEEN REWRITTEN TO SPEED UP THE LOCATION OF 
7397     !C              OF ROWS WHICH ARE TO BE ELIMINATED.  THIS IS DONE BY 
7398     !C              FIRST STORING THE LARGEST ELEMENT OF EACH ROW IN     
7399     !C              THE ARRAY RW.  THE DIAGONAL ENTRY IS THEN COMPARED   
7400     !C              WITH THE CORRESPONDING ELEMENT IN RW.  IF IT IS      
7401     !C              DECIDED TO ELIMINATE THE ROW THEN IT IS MARKED FOR   
7402     !C              ELIMINATION. 
7403     !C       
7404     !C              WHEN A ROW IS TO BE ELIMINATED ITS DIAGONAL ENTRY    
7405     !C              IS STORED IN  RW  AND  IW IS MARKED BY A NONZERO     
7406     !C              (WHICH IS THIS ROW NUMBER)       
7407     !C       
7408     !C              ROWS WHICH HAVE ONLY DIAGONAL ENTRIES ARE NOT
7409     !C              ALTERED.     
7410     !C       
7411     !C*********************************************************************
7412     !C       
7413     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR ARGUMENTS    
7414     !C       
7415     !      INTEGER NN,IA(1),JA(1),IW(NN),ISYM,LEVEL,NOUT,IER   
7416     !      DOUBLE PRECISION A(1),RHS(NN),RW(NN),TOL  
7417     !C       
7418     !C ... SPECIFICATIONS FOR LOCAL VARIABLES
7419     !C       
7420     !      INTEGER IBGN,ICNT,IEND,JJ,JJDI,KK,N       
7421     !      DOUBLE PRECISION DI   
7422     !C       
7423     !      N = NN      
7424     !C       
7425     !C        IF (N .GE. 1) GO TO 10       
7426     !C           IER = 100       
7427     !C           RETURN
7428     !C 10     CONTINUE 
7429     !C       
7430     !C ... STORE THE LARGEST (DABSOLUTE VALUE) OFF DIAGONAL ENTRY FOR    
7431     !C ... ROW II IN RW(II).     
7432     !C       
7433     !      IER = 0     
7434     !      ICNT = 0    
7435     !      DO 10 II = 1,N
7436     !         RW(II) = 0.0D0     
7437     !         IW(II) = 0 
7438     !   10 CONTINUE    
7439     !      DO 20 II = 1,N
7440     !         IBGN = IA(II)      
7441     !         IEND = IA(II+1)-1  
7442     !         IF (IBGN.GT.IEND) GO TO 140  
7443     !         DO 20 JJ = IBGN,IEND 
7444     !            KK = JA(JJ)     
7445     !            IF (KK.EQ.II) GO TO 20    
7446     !            RW(II) = DMAX1(RW(II),DABS(A(JJ)))  
7447     !            IF (ISYM.NE.0) GO TO 20   
7448     !            RW(KK) = DMAX1(RW(KK),DABS(A(JJ)))  
7449     !   20 CONTINUE    
7450     !C       
7451     !C ... FOR II = 1 TO N FIND THE DIAGONAL ENTRY IN ROW II   
7452     !C       
7453     !      DO 80 II = 1,N
7454     !         IBGN = IA(II)      
7455     !         IEND = IA(II+1)-1  
7456     !         DO 40 JJ = IBGN,IEND 
7457     !            IF (JA(JJ).NE.II) GO TO 40
7458     !            DI = A(JJ)      
7459     !            JJDI = JJ       
7460     !            IF (DI.GT.0.D0) GO TO 50  
7461     !            IER = 101       
7462     !            IF (LEVEL.GE.0) WRITE (NOUT,30) II,DI 
7463     !   30       FORMAT ('0','*** F A T A L     E R R O R ************'/'0', 
7464     !     *         '    IN ITPACK ROUTINE SBELM   '/' ',      
7465     !     *         '    DIAGONAL ELEMENT',I10,' NOT POSITIVE  '/' ',    
7466     !     *         '    CURRENT VALUE = ',D15.8)    
7467     !            RETURN
7468     !   40    CONTINUE 
7469     !         GO TO 140
7470     !   50    CONTINUE 
7471     !C       
7472     !C ... CHECK THE SIZE OF THE LARGEST OFF DIAGONAL ELEMENT  
7473     !C ... ( STORED IN RW(II) ) AGAINST THE DIAGONAL ELEMENT DII.
7474     !C       
7475     !         IF (RW(II).NE.0.0D0) GO TO 60
7476     !         IF (1.0D0/DI.LE.TOL) GO TO 70
7477     !         GO TO 80 
7478     !   60    IF (RW(II)/DI.GT.TOL) GO TO 80 
7479     !C       
7480     !C ... THE OFF DIAGONAL ELEMENTS ARE SMALL COMPARED TO THE DIAGONAL  
7481     !C ... THEREFORE MARK IT FOR ELIMINATION AND PERFORM INITIAL 
7482     !C ... PROCESSING  
7483     !C       
7484     !   70    ICNT = ICNT+1      
7485     !         IW(II) = II
7486     !         RW(II) = DI
7487     !         A(JJDI) = 1.0D0    
7488     !         RHS(II) = RHS(II)/DI 
7489     !C       
7490     !   80 CONTINUE    
7491     !C       
7492     !C ... ELIMINATE THE ROWS AND COLUMNS INDICATED BY THE NONZERO       
7493     !C ... ENTRIES IN IW.  THERE ARE ICNT OF THEM    
7494     !C       
7495     !      IF (ICNT.EQ.0) GO TO 130
7496     !C       
7497     !C ... THE ELIMINATION IS AS FOLLOWS:  
7498     !C       
7499     !C     FOR II = 1 TO N DO    
7500     !C        IF ( IW(II) .NE. 0 ) THEN    
7501     !C           SET DIAGONAL VALUE TO 1.0  ( ALREADY DONE )   
7502     !C           SET RHS(II) = RHS(II) / RW(II)   ( ALREADY DONE )       
7503     !C           FIND NONZERO OFFDIAGONAL ENTRIES  KK
7504     !C           IF ( IW(KK) .EQ. 0 ) FIX UP RHS(KK)  WHEN USING SYMMETRIC ST
7505     !C           SET A(II,KK) = 0.0
7506     !C        ELSE ( I.E.  IW(II) .EQ. 0  )
7507     !C           FIND NONZERO OFFDIAGONAL ENTRIES   KK 
7508     !C           IF ( IW(KK) .NE. 0 ) FIX UP RHS(II) 
7509     !C                                AND SET A(II,KK) = 0.0   
7510     !C        END IF   
7511     !C     END DO      
7512     !C       
7513     !      DO 120 II = 1,N       
7514     !         IBGN = IA(II)      
7515     !         IEND = IA(II+1)-1  
7516     !         IF (IW(II).EQ.0) GO TO 100   
7517     !C       
7518     !C ... THE II-TH ROW IS TO BE ELIMINATED 
7519     !C       
7520     !         DO 90 JJ = IBGN,IEND 
7521     !            KK = JA(JJ)     
7522     !            IF (KK.EQ.II) GO TO 90    
7523     !            IF ((IW(KK).EQ.0).AND.(ISYM.EQ.0)) RHS(KK) = RHS(KK)-A(JJ)* 
7524     !     *         RHS(II)      
7525     !            A(JJ) = 0.0D0   
7526     !   90    CONTINUE 
7527     !         GO TO 120
7528     !C       
7529     !C ... THE II-TH ROW IS KEPT.  CHECK THE OFF-DIAGONAL ENTRIES
7530     !C       
7531     !  100    DO 110 JJ = IBGN,IEND
7532     !            KK = JA(JJ)     
7533     !            IF (KK.EQ.II.OR.IW(KK).EQ.0) GO TO 110
7534     !            RHS(II) = RHS(II)-A(JJ)*RHS(KK)     
7535     !            A(JJ) = 0.0D0   
7536     !  110    CONTINUE 
7537     !C       
7538     !  120 CONTINUE    
7539     !C       
7540     !  130 RETURN      
7541     !C       
7542     !C ... ERROR TRAPS -- NO DIAGONAL ENTRY IN ROW II (ROW MAY BE EMPTY).
7543     !C       
7544     !  140 CONTINUE    
7545     !      IER = 102   
7546     !      IF (LEVEL.GE.0) WRITE (NOUT,150) II       
7547     !  150 FORMAT ('0','*** F A T A L     E R R O R ************'/'0',   
7548     !     *   '    IN ITPACK ROUTINE SBELM   '/' ',  
7549     !     *   '    NO DIAGONAL ENTRY IN ROW  ',I10)  
7550     !C       
7551     !      RETURN      
7552     !      END 
7553     !      SUBROUTINE SBEND (N,NZ,IA,JA,A,IWORK)     
7554     !C       
7555     !C***********************************************************************
7556     !C       
7557     !C     SBEND IS THE THIRD OF A SUITE OF SUBROUTINES TO AID THE       
7558     !C     USER TO CONSTRUCT THE  IA, JA, A DATA STRUCTURE USED IN       
7559     !C     ITPACK.     
7560     !C       
7561     !C     SBEND RESTRUCTURES THE LINKED LIST DATA STRUCTURE BUILT BY    
7562     !C     SBINI AND SBSIJ INTO THE FINAL DATA STRUCTURE REQUIRE BY      
7563     !C     ITPACK.  THE RESTRUCTURING CAN TAKE PLACE IN THE MINIMUM      
7564     !C     AMOUNT OF MEMORY REQUIRED TO HOLD THE NONZERO STRUCTURE OF    
7565     !C     THE SPARSE MATRIX BUT WILL RUN QUICKER IF MORE STORAGE
7566     !C     IS ALLOWED. 
7567     !C       
7568     !C     SBEND IS BASED ON SUBROUTINE BUILD OF THE SPARSE MATRIX       
7569     !C     PACKAGE SPARSPAK DEVELOPED BY ALAN GEORGE AND JOSEPH LUI      
7570     !C     OF THE UNIVERSITY OF WATERLOO, WATERLOO, ONTARIO.   
7571     !C       
7572     !C ... PARAMETERS  
7573     !C       
7574     !C ...... INPUT    
7575     !C       
7576     !C     N       THE ORDER OF THE LINEAR SYSTEM    
7577     !C       
7578     !C     NZ      THE LENGTH OF THE ARRAYS JA, IWORK, AND A.  
7579     !C       
7580     !C ...... INPUT/OUTPUT       
7581     !C       
7582     !C     IA      INTEGER ARRAY OF LENGTH N+1.  THE FIRST N ENTRIES     
7583     !C             POINT TO THE BEGINNING OF THE LINKED LIST FOR EACH    
7584     !C             ROW.  IA(N+1)-1 IS THE TOP OF THE LINKED LISTS
7585     !C             CONTAINED IN JA, IWORK, AND A.  ON OUTPUT IA WILL     
7586     !C             POINT TO THE FIRST ENTRY OF EACH ROW IN THE FINAL     
7587     !C             DATA STRUCTURE. 
7588     !C       
7589     !C     JA      INTEGER ARRAY OF LENGTH NZ.  ON INPUT JA STORES THE   
7590     !C             COLUMN NUMBERS OF THE NONZERO ENTRIES AS INDICATED    
7591     !C             BY THE LINKED LISTS.  ON OUTPUT JA STORES THE 
7592     !C             COLUMN NUMBERS IN ROW ORDERED FORM. 
7593     !C       
7594     !C     A       D.P. ARRAY OF LENGTH NZ.  ON INPUT A STORES THE       
7595     !C             VALUE OF THE NOZERO ENTRIES AS INDICATED BY THE       
7596     !C             LINKED LISTS.  ON OUTPUT A STORES THE VALUES IN       
7597     !C             ROW ORDERED FORM.       
7598     !C       
7599     !C     IWORK    INTEGER ARRAY OF LENGTH NZ.  ON INPUT IWORK STORES THE 
7600     !C             THE LINKS OF THE LINKED LISTS.  ON OUTPUT IT IS       
7601     !C             DESTROYED.    
7602     !C       
7603     !C***********************************************************************
7604     !C       
7605     !      INTEGER N,NZ,IA(1),JA(NZ),IWORK(NZ)       
7606     !      DOUBLE PRECISION A(NZ)
7607     !C       
7608     !      INTEGER MAXTOP,NEXT,TOP,IDEG,NULINK,JAJ,HLINK,OHLINK,L,I,LINK,
7609     !     *   MHLINK   
7610     !      DOUBLE PRECISION VAL  
7611     !C       
7612     !C***********************************************************************
7613     !C       
7614     !C ... INITIALIZATION
7615     !C       
7616     !C ...... THE VARIABLES NEXT AND TOP RESPECTIVELY POINT TO THE       
7617     !C        NEXT AVAILABLE ENTRY FOR THE FINAL DATA STRUCTURE AND      
7618     !C        THE TOP OF THE REMAINDER OF THE LINKED LISTS.    
7619     !C       
7620     !      NEXT = 1    
7621     !      TOP = IA(N+1)+1       
7622     !      MAXTOP = NZ-IA(N+1)+1 
7623     !C       
7624     !C***********************************************************************
7625     !C       
7626     !C ... CONVERT EACH ROW INTO FINAL FORM
7627     !C       
7628     !      DO 90 I = 1,N 
7629     !         IDEG = 0 
7630     !         NULINK = IA(I)     
7631     !C       
7632     !C ... LOOP OVER EACH NODE IN THE LINKED LIST OF ROW I     
7633     !C       
7634     !   10    LINK = NULINK      
7635     !         IF (LINK.LE.0) GO TO 80      
7636     !         NULINK = IWORK(LINK) 
7637     !         JAJ = JA(LINK)     
7638     !         VAL = A(LINK)      
7639     !C       
7640     !C ... CHECK TO SEE IF A COLLISION BETWEEN THE LINKED LISTS
7641     !C     AND THE FINAL FORM HAS OCCURRED.
7642     !C       
7643     !         IF (NEXT.GE.TOP.AND.LINK.NE.TOP) GO TO 20
7644     !C       
7645     !C ... COLLISION HAS NOT OCCURRED.  FREE THE SPACE FOR THE TRIPLE    
7646     !C     (JA(LINK), A(LINK), IWORK(LINK))
7647     !C       
7648     !         JA(LINK) = 0       
7649     !         A(LINK) = 0.0D0    
7650     !         IWORK(LINK) = 0    
7651     !C       
7652     !C ... SPECIAL CASE TO MOVE  TOP  DOWN IF LINK .EQ. TOP    
7653     !C       
7654     !         IF (LINK.EQ.TOP) GO TO 60    
7655     !         GO TO 70 
7656     !C       
7657     !C***********************************************************************
7658     !C       
7659     !C ... COLLISION HAS OCCURRED.  CLEAR OFF SOME SPACE FOR THE CURRENT 
7660     !C     ENTRY BY MOVING THE TRIPLE ( JA(TOP),A(TOP),IWORK(TOP) )      
7661     !C     DOWNWARDS TO THE FREED TRIPLE ( JA(LINK),A(LINK),IWORK(LINK) ). 
7662     !C     THEN ADJUST THE LINK FIELDS.    
7663     !C       
7664     !C ...... PATCH UP THE LINKED LIST FOR THE CURRENT ROW I.  THEN      
7665     !C        TRAVERSE THE LINKED LIST CONTAINING TOP UNTIL THE POINTER  
7666     !C        POINTER BACK TO IA IS FOUND. 
7667     !C       
7668     !   20    IA(I) = LINK       
7669     !         HLINK = TOP
7670     !C       
7671     !   30    HLINK = IWORK(HLINK) 
7672     !         IF (HLINK.GT.0) GO TO 30     
7673     !C       
7674     !C ...... NOW FOLLOW THE LINKED LIST BACK TO TOP KEEPING TRACK       
7675     !C        OF THE OLD LINK.   
7676     !C       
7677     !C ......... SPECIAL CASE IF IA(-HLINK) = TOP    
7678     !C       
7679     !         MHLINK = -HLINK    
7680     !         IF (IA(MHLINK).NE.TOP) GO TO 40
7681     !C       
7682     !         IWORK(LINK) = IWORK(TOP)     
7683     !         JA(LINK) = JA(TOP) 
7684     !         A(LINK) = A(TOP)   
7685     !         IA(MHLINK) = LINK  
7686     !         IF (NULINK.EQ.TOP) NULINK = LINK       
7687     !         GO TO 60 
7688     !C       
7689     !C ......... USUAL CASE.     
7690     !C       
7691     !   40    HLINK = IA(MHLINK) 
7692     !   50    OHLINK = HLINK     
7693     !         HLINK = IWORK(OHLINK)
7694     !         IF (HLINK.NE.TOP) GO TO 50   
7695     !C       
7696     !         IWORK(LINK) = IWORK(TOP)     
7697     !         JA(LINK) = JA(TOP) 
7698     !         A(LINK) = A(TOP)   
7699     !         IF (OHLINK.NE.LINK) IWORK(OHLINK) = LINK 
7700     !         IF (NULINK.EQ.TOP) NULINK = LINK       
7701     !C       
7702     !C ... COLLAPSE TOP OF LINK LIST BY AS MUCH AS POSSIBLE    
7703     !C       
7704     !   60    TOP = TOP+1
7705     !         IF (TOP.GE.MAXTOP) GO TO 70  
7706     !         IF (IWORK(TOP).NE.0) GO TO 70
7707     !         GO TO 60 
7708     !C       
7709     !C***********************************************************************
7710     !C       
7711     !C ... PUT THE CURRENT TRIPLE INTO THE FINAL DATA STRUCTURE
7712     !C       
7713     !   70    JA(NEXT) = JAJ     
7714     !         A(NEXT) = VAL      
7715     !         NEXT = NEXT+1      
7716     !         IDEG = IDEG+1      
7717     !         GO TO 10 
7718     !C       
7719     !C ... FINAL STRUCTURE FOR ROW I IS COMPLETE.  LINKED LIST IS
7720     !C     DESTROYED AND WILL BE RECAPTURED AS NECESSARY BY THE
7721     !C     LOOP ON LABEL 60      
7722     !C       
7723     !   80    IA(I) = IDEG       
7724     !C       
7725     !   90 CONTINUE    
7726     !C       
7727     !C***********************************************************************
7728     !C       
7729     !C ... FINALIZE THE DATA STRUCTURE BY BUILDING THE FINAL VERSION OF  
7730     !C     IA. 
7731     !C       
7732     !      L = IA(1)+1 
7733     !      IA(1) = 1   
7734     !      DO 100 I = 1,N
7735     !         IDEG = IA(I+1)     
7736     !         IA(I+1) = L
7737     !         L = L+IDEG 
7738     !  100 CONTINUE    
7739     !C       
7740     !C ... FINAL IA, JA, A DATA STRUCTURE BUILT.     
7741     !C       
7742     !      RETURN      
7743     !      END 
7744     !      SUBROUTINE SBINI (N,NZ,IA,JA,A,IWORK)     
7745     !C       
7746     !C***********************************************************************
7747     !C       
7748     !C     SBINI IS THE FIRST OF A SUITE OF THREE SUBROUTINES TO AID     
7749     !C     THE USER TO CONSTRUCT THE IA, JA, A DATA STRUCTURE USED       
7750     !C     IN ITPACK.  
7751     !C       
7752     !C     SBINI INITIALIZES THE ARRAYS IA, JA, IWORK, AND A.  THE OTHER 
7753     !C     SUBROUTINES IN THE SUITE ARE SBSIJ ( WHICH BUILDS A LINKED    
7754     !C     LIST REPRESENTATION OF THE MATRIX STRUCTURE ) AND SBEND ( WHICH 
7755     !C     RESTRUCTURE THE LINKED LIST FORM INTO THE FINAL FORM ).       
7756     !C       
7757     !C ... PARAMETERS  
7758     !C       
7759     !C ...... INPUT    
7760     !C       
7761     !C     N          THE ORDER OF THE LINEAR SYSTEM 
7762     !C       
7763     !C     NZ         THE MAXIMUM NUMBER OF NONZEROES ALLOWED IN THE     
7764     !C                LINEAR SYSTEM.       
7765     !C       
7766     !C ...... OUTPUT   
7767     !C       
7768     !C     IA         INTEGER ARRAY OF LENGTH N+1.  SBINI SETS THIS ARRAY
7769     !C                TO -I FOR I = 1 THRU N.  IA(N+1) IS SET TO NZ.     
7770     !C       
7771     !C     JA         INTEGER ARRAY OF LENGTH NZ.  INITIALIZED TO ZERO HERE. 
7772     !C       
7773     !C     A          D.P. ARRAY OF LENGTH NZ.  INITIALIZED TO ZERO HERE.
7774     !C       
7775     !C     IWORK       INTEGER ARRAY OF LENGTH NZ.  INITIALIZED TO ZERO HERE.
7776     !C       
7777     !C***********************************************************************
7778     !C       
7779     !      INTEGER N,NZ,IA(1),JA(NZ),IWORK(NZ),I     
7780     !      DOUBLE PRECISION A(NZ)
7781     !C       
7782     !C***********************************************************************
7783     !C       
7784     !      DO 10 I = 1,N 
7785     !         IA(I) = -I 
7786     !   10 CONTINUE    
7787     !      IA(N+1) = NZ
7788     !C       
7789     !      CALL IVFILL (NZ,JA,0) 
7790     !      CALL IVFILL (NZ,IWORK,0)
7791     !      CALL VFILL (NZ,A,0.D0)
7792     !C       
7793     !      RETURN      
7794     !      END 
7795     !      SUBROUTINE SBSIJ (N,NZ,IA,JA,A,IWORK,II,JJ,VALL,MODE,LEVELL,NOUTT,
7796     !     *   IERR)    
7797     !C       
7798     !C***********************************************************************
7799     !C       
7800     !C     SBSIJ IS THE SECOND OF A SUITE OF THREE SUBROUTINES TO AID IN 
7801     !C     THE CONSTRUCTION OF THE IA, JA, A DATA STRUCTURE USED IN      
7802     !C     ITPACK.     
7803     !C       
7804     !C     SBSIJ TAKES THE INDIVIDUAL ENTRIES OF THE SPARSE MATRIX AS    
7805     !C     GIVEN TO IT AT EACH CALL VIA  (I,J,VAL) AND INSERTS IT INTO   
7806     !C     A LINKED LIST REPRESENTATION OF THE SPARSE MATRIX.  
7807     !C       
7808     !C     EACH ROW OF THE SPARSE MATRIX IS ASSOCIATED WITH A CIRCULAR   
7809     !C     LINKED LIST BEGINNING AT IA(I).  THE LAST ENTERED ELEMENT IN  
7810     !C     EACH LIST POINTS BACK TO IA(I) WITH THE VALUE -I.  THE LINKS  
7811     !C     ARE STORED IN THE ARRAY IWORK, WHILE JA AND A STORE THE COLUMN
7812     !C     NUMBER AND VALUE IN PARALLEL TO IWORK.  THE LINKED LISTED ARE 
7813     !C     STORED BEGINNING AT ENTRY NZ AND WORKING BACKWARDS TOWARDS 1. 
7814     !C       
7815     !C ... PARAMETERS  
7816     !C       
7817     !C ...... INPUT    
7818     !C       
7819     !C     N       THE ORDER OF THE LINEAR SYSTEM    
7820     !C       
7821     !C     NZ      THE LENGTH OF THE ARRAYS  JA, A, AND IWORK  
7822     !C       
7823     !C     I, J    THE ROW AND COLUMN NUMBERS OF THE ENTRY OF THE SPARSE 
7824     !C             LINEAR SYSTEM TO BE ENTERED IN THE DATA STRUCTURE(=II,JJ) 
7825     !C       
7826     !C     VAL     THE NONZERO VALUE ASSOCIATED WITH (I,J)  (= VALL)     
7827     !C       
7828     !C     MODE    IF THE (I,J) ENTRY HAS ALREADY BEEN SET, MODE SPECIFIES 
7829     !C             THE WAY IN WHICH THE ENTRY IS TO BE TREATED.
7830     !C             IF   MODE .LT. 0  LET THE VALUE REMAIN AS IS
7831     !C                       .EQ. 0  RESET IT TO THE NEW VALUE 
7832     !C                       .GT. 0  ADD THE NEW VALUE TO THE OLD VALUE  
7833     !C       
7834     !C     NOUT  OUTPUT FILE NUMBER (= NOUTT)
7835     !C       
7836     !C     LEVEL   OUTPUT FILE SWITCH (= LEVELL)     
7837     !C ... INPUT/OUTPUT
7838     !C       
7839     !C     IA      INTEGER ARRAY OF LENGTH N+1.  THE FIRST N ENTRIES     
7840     !C             POINT TO THE BEGINNING OF THE LINKED LIST FOR EACH    
7841     !C             ROW.  IA(N+1) POINTS TO THE NEXT ENTRY AVAILABLE FOR  
7842     !C             STORING THE CURRENT ENTRY INTO THE LINKED LIST.       
7843     !C       
7844     !C     JA      INTEGER ARRAY OF LENGTH NZ.  JA STORES THE COLUMN     
7845     !C             NUMBERS OF THE NONZERO ENTRIES.   
7846     !C       
7847     !C     A       D.P. ARRAY OF LENGTH NZ.  A STORES THE VALUE OF THE   
7848     !C             NONZERO ENTRIES.
7849     !C       
7850     !C     IWORK   INTEGER ARRAY OF LENGTH NZ. IWORK STORES THE LINKS.   
7851     !C       
7852     !C     IER     ERROR FLAG.(= IERR)  POSSIBLE RETURNS ARE   
7853     !C             IER =    0   SUCCESSFUL COMPLETION
7854     !C                 =  700   ENTRY WAS ALREADY SET,  VALUE HANDLED    
7855     !C                          AS SPECIFIED BY MODE.

7969     !      SUBROUTINE SCAL (NN,IA,JA,A,RHS,U,D,LEVEL,NOUT,IER) 
7970     !C       
7971     !C ... ORIGINAL MATRIX IS SCALED TO A UNIT DIAGONAL MATRIX.  RHS     
7972     !C ... AND U ARE SCALED ACCORDINGLY.  THE MATRIX IS THEN SPLIT AND

8033     !   70    CONTINUE

8245     !      SUBROUTINE UNSCAL (N,IA,JA,A,RHS,U,D)

8312     !      SUBROUTINE VEVMW (N,V,W)
8313     !C       
8314     !C ... VEVMW COMPUTES V = V - W
8315     !C       
8316     !C ... PARAMETER LIST:       
8317     !C       
8318     !C          N      INTEGER LENGTH OF VECTORS V AND W       
8319     !C          V      D.P. VECTOR

8321     !C

8514     !      SUBROUTINE ZBRENT (N,TRI,EPS,NSIG,AA,BB,MAXFNN,IER) 
8515     !C       
8516     !C   MODIFIED IMSL ROUTINE NAME   - ZBRENT       
8517     !C       
8518     !C-----------------------------------------------------------------------
8519     !C       
8520     !C   COMPUTER            - CDC/SINGLE  
8521     !C       
8522     !C   LATEST REVISION     - JANUARY 1, 1978       
8523     !C       
8524     !C   PURPOSE             - ZERO OF A FUNCTION WHICH CHANGES SIGN IN A
8525     !C                           GIVEN INTERVAL (BRENT ALGORITHM)
8526     !C       
8527     !C   USAGE               - CALL ZBRENT (F,EPS,NSIG,A,B,MAXFN,IER)    
8528     !C       
8529     !C   ARGUMENTS    TRI    - A TRIDIAGONAL MATRIX OF ORDER N 
8530     !C                EPS    - FIRST CONVERGENCE CRITERION (INPUT).  A ROOT, 
8531     !C                           B, IS ACCEPTED IF DABS(F(B)) IS LESS THAN OR
8532     !C                           EQUAL TO EPS.  EPS MAY BE SET TO ZERO.  
8533     !C                NSIG   - SECOND CONVERGENCE CRITERION (INPUT).  A ROOT,
8534     !C                           B, IS ACCEPTED IF THE CURRENT APPROXIMATION 
8535     !C                           AGREES WITH THE TRUE SOLUTION TO NSIG   
8536     !C                           SIGNIFICANT DIGITS. 
8537     !C                A,B    - ON INPUT, THE USER MUST SUPPLY TWO POINTS, A
8538     !C                           AND B, SUCH THAT F(A) AND F(B) ARE OPPOSITE 
8539     !C                           IN SIGN. (= AA, BB) 
8540     !C                           ON OUTPUT, BOTH A AND B ARE ALTERED.  B 
8541     !C                           WILL CONTAIN THE BEST APPROXIMATION TO THE
8542     !C                           ROOT OF F. SEE REMARK 1.      
8543     !C                MAXFN  - ON INPUT, MAXFN SHOULD CONTAIN AN UPPER BOUND 
8544     !C                           ON THE NUMBER OF FUNCTION EVALUATIONS   
8545     !C                           REQUIRED FOR CONVERGENCE.  ON OUTPUT, MAXFN 
8546     !C                           WILL CONTAIN THE ACTUAL NUMBER OF FUNCTION
8547     !C                           EVALUATIONS USED. (= MAXFNN)  
8548     !C                IER    - ERROR PARAMETER. (OUTPUT)       
8549     !C                         TERMINAL ERROR
8550     !C                           IER = 501 INDICATES THE ALGORITHM FAILED TO 
8551     !C                             CONVERGE IN MAXFN EVALUATIONS.
8552     !C                           IER = 502 INDICATES F(A) AND F(B) HAVE THE
8553     !C                             SAME SIGN.
8554     !C       
8555     !C   PRECISION/HARDWARE  - SINGLE AND DOUBLE/H32 
8556     !C                       - SINGLE/H36,H48,H60    
8557     !C       
8558     !C   NOTATION            - INFORMATION ON SPECIAL NOTATION AND       
8559     !C                           CONVENTIONS IS AVAILABLE IN THE MANUAL  
8560     !C                           INTRODUCTION OR THROUGH IMSL ROUTINE UHELP
8561     !C       
8562     !C   REMARKS  1.  LET F(X) BE THE CHARACTERISTIC FUNCTION OF THE MATRIX
8563     !C                TRI EVALUATED AT X. FUNCTION DETERM EVALUATES F(X).
8564     !C                ON EXIT FROM ZBRENT, WHEN IER=0, A AND B SATISFY THE 
8565     !C                FOLLOWING, 
8566     !C                F(A)*F(B) .LE.0,     
8567     !C                DABS(F(B)) .LE. DABS(F(A)), AND
8568     !C                EITHER DABS(F(B)) .LE. EPS OR  
8569     !C                DABS(A-B) .LE. MAX(DABS(B),0.1)*10.0**(-NSIG).     
8570     !C                THE PRESENCE OF 0.1 IN THIS ERROR CRITERION CAUSES 
8571     !C                LEADING ZEROES TO THE RIGHT OF THE DECIMAL POINT TO BE 
8572     !C                COUNTED AS SIGNIFICANT DIGITS. SCALING MAY BE REQUIRED 
8573     !C                IN ORDER TO ACCURATELY DETERMINE A ZERO OF SMALL   
8574     !C                MAGNITUDE. 
8575     !C            2.  ZBRENT IS GUARANTEED TO REACH CONVERGENCE WITHIN   
8576     !C                K = (DLOG((B-A)/D)+1.0)**2 FUNCTION EVALUATIONS WHERE
8577     !C                  D=MIN(OVER X IN (A,B) OF     
8578     !C                    MAX(DABS(X),0.1)*10.0**(-NSIG)).     
8579     !C                THIS IS AN UPPER BOUND ON THE NUMBER OF EVALUATIONS. 
8580     !C                RARELY DOES THE ACTUAL NUMBER OF EVALUATIONS USED BY 
8581     !C                ZBRENT EXCEED DSQRT(K). D CAN BE COMPUTED AS FOLLOWS,
8582     !C                  P = DBLE(AMIN1(DABS(A),DABS(B)))       
8583     !C                  P = DMAX1(0.1,P)   
8584     !C                  IF ((A-0.1)*(B-0.1).LT.0.0) P = 0.1    
8585     !C                  D = P*10.0**(-NSIG)
8586     !C       
8587     !C   COPYRIGHT           - 1977 BY IMSL, INC. ALL RIGHTS RESERVED.   
8588     !C       
8589     !C   WARRANTY            - IMSL WARRANTS ONLY THAT IMSL TESTING HAS BEEN 
8590     !C                           APPLIED TO THIS CODE. NO OTHER WARRANTY,
8591     !C                           EXPRESSED OR IMPLIED, IS APPLICABLE.    
8592     !C       
8593     !C-----------------------------------------------------------------------
8594     !C       
8595     !C *** BEGIN: ITPACK COMMON  
8596     !C       
8597     !      INTEGER IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT       
8598     !      COMMON /ITCOM1/ IN,IS,ISYM,ITMAX,LEVEL,NOUT 
8599     !C       
8600     !      LOGICAL ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD   
8601     !      COMMON /ITCOM2/ ADAPT,BETADT,CASEII,HALT,PARTAD     
8602     !C       
8603     !      DOUBLE PRECISION BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA,
8604     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
8605     !      COMMON /ITCOM3/ BDELNM,BETAB,CME,DELNNM,DELSNM,FF,GAMMA,OMEGA,QA, 
8606     !     *   QT,RHO,RRR,SIGE,SME,SPECR,SPR,DRELPR,STPTST,UDNM,ZETA      
8607     !C       
8608     !C *** END  : ITPACK COMMON  
8609     !C       
8610     !C     DESCRIPTION OF VARIABLES IN COMMON BLOCK IN MAIN SUBROUTINE   
8611     !C       
8612     !C                                  SPECIFICATIONS FOR ARGUMENTS     
8613     !C       
8614     !      INTEGER NSIG,MAXFNN,IER 
8615     !      DOUBLE PRECISION TRI(2,1),EPS,AA,BB       
8616     !C       
8617     !C                                  SPECIFICATIONS FOR LOCAL VARIABLES 
8618     !C       
8619     !      INTEGER IC,MAXFN      
8620     !      DOUBLE PRECISION ZERO,HALF,ONE,THREE,TEN,A,B,T,FA,FB,C,FC,D,E,TOL,
8621     !     *   RM,S,P,Q,R,RONE,TEMP,DETERM  
8622     !      DATA ZERO / 0.D0 / ,HALF / 5.D-1 / ,ONE / 1.D0 / ,THREE / 3.D0 / ,
8623     !     *   TEN / 10.D0 /      
8624     !C       
8625     !C                                  FIRST EXECUTABLE STATEMENT       
8626     !C       
8627     !      A = AA      
8628     !      B = BB      
8629     !      MAXFN = MAXFNN
8630     !      IER = 0     
8631     !      T = TEN**(-NSIG)      
8632     !      IC = 2      
8633     !      FA = DETERM(N,TRI,A)  
8634     !      FB = DETERM(N,TRI,B)  
8635     !      S = B       
8636     !C       
8637     !C                                  TEST FOR SAME SIGN     
8638     !C       
8639     !      IF (FA*FB.GT.ZERO) GO TO 110    
8640     !   10 C = A       
8641     !      FC = FA     
8642     !      D = B-C     
8643     !      E = D       
8644     !   20 IF (DABS(FC).GE.DABS(FB)) GO TO 30
8645     !      A = B       
8646     !      B = C       
8647     !      C = A       
8648     !      FA = FB     
8649     !      FB = FC     
8650     !      FC = FA     
8651     !   30 CONTINUE    
8652     !      TOL = T*DMAX1(DABS(B),0.1D0)    
8653     !      RM = (C-B)*HALF       
8654     !C       
8655     !C                                  TEST FOR FIRST CONVERGENCE CRITERIA
8656     !C       
8657     !      IF (DABS(FB).LE.EPS) GO TO 80   
8658     !C       
8659     !C                                  TEST FOR SECOND CONVERGENCE CRITERIA 
8660     !C       
8661     !      IF (DABS(C-B).LE.TOL) GO TO 80  
8662     !C       
8663     !C                                  CHECK EVALUATION COUNTER 
8664     !C       
8665     !      IF (IC.GE.MAXFN) GO TO 90       
8666     !C       
8667     !C                                  IS BISECTION FORCED    
8668     !C       
8669     !      IF (DABS(E).LT.TOL) GO TO 60    
8670     !      IF (DABS(FA).LE.DABS(FB)) GO TO 60
8671     !      S = FB/FA   
8672     !      IF (A.NE.C) GO TO 40  
8673     !C       
8674     !C                                  LINEAR INTERPOLATION   
8675     !C       
8676     !      P = (C-B)*S 
8677     !      Q = ONE-S   
8678     !      GO TO 50    
8679     !C       
8680     !C                                  INVERSE QUADRATIC INTERPOLATION  
8681     !C       
8682     !   40 Q = FA/FC   
8683     !      R = FB/FC   
8684     !      RONE = R-ONE
8685     !      P = S*((C-B)*Q*(Q-R)-(B-A)*RONE)
8686     !      Q = (Q-ONE)*RONE*(S-ONE)
8687     !   50 IF (P.GT.ZERO) Q = -Q 
8688     !      IF (P.LT.ZERO) P = -P 
8689     !      S = E       
8690     !      E = D       
8691     !C       
8692     !C                                  IF DABS(P/Q).GE.75*DABS(C-B) THEN
8693     !C                                     FORCE BISECTION     
8694     !C       
8695     !      IF (P+P.GE.THREE*RM*Q) GO TO 60 
8696     !C       
8697     !C                                  IF DABS(P/Q).GE..5*DABS(S) THEN FORCE
8698     !C                                     BISECTION. S = THE VALUE OF P/Q 
8699     !C                                     ON THE STEP BEFORE THE LAST ONE 
8700     !C       
8701     !      IF (P+P.GE.DABS(S*Q)) GO TO 60  
8702     !      D = P/Q     
8703     !      GO TO 70    
8704     !C       
8705     !C                                  BISECTION    
8706     !C       
8707     !   60 E = RM      
8708     !      D = E       
8709     !C       
8710     !C                                  INCREMENT B  
8711     !C       
8712     !   70 A = B       
8713     !      FA = FB     
8714     !      TEMP = D    
8715     !      IF (DABS(TEMP).LE.HALF*TOL) TEMP = DSIGN(HALF*TOL,RM) 
8716     !      B = B+TEMP  
8717     !      S = B       
8718     !      FB = DETERM(N,TRI,S)  
8719     !      IC = IC+1   
8720     !      IF (FB*FC.LE.ZERO) GO TO 20     
8721     !      GO TO 10    
8722     !C       
8723     !C                                  CONVERGENCE OF B       
8724     !C       
8725     !   80 A = C       
8726     !      MAXFN = IC  
8727     !      GO TO 130   
8728     !C       
8729     !C                                  MAXFN EVALUATIONS      
8730     !C       
8731     !   90 IER = 501   
8732     !      A = C       
8733     !      MAXFN = IC  
8734     !      IF (LEVEL.GE.1) WRITE (NOUT,100) MAXFN    
8735     !  100 FORMAT ('0','*** W A R N I N G ************'/'0',   
8736     !     *   '    IN ITPACK ROUTINE ZBRENT  '/' ',  
8737     !     *   '    ALGORITHM FAILED TO CONVERGE   '/' ','    IN',I6,     
8738     !     *   ' ITERATIONS ')    
8739     !      GO TO 130   
8740     !C       
8741     !C                                  TERMINAL ERROR - F(A) AND F(B) HAVE
8742     !C                                  THE SAME SIGN
8743     !C       
8744     !  110 IER = 502   
8745     !      MAXFN = IC  
8746     !      IF (LEVEL.GE.1) WRITE (NOUT,120)
8747     !  120 FORMAT ('0','*** W A R N I N G ************'/'0',   
8748     !     *   '    IN ITPACK ROUTINE ZBRENT  '/' ',  
8749     !     *   '    F(A) AND F(B) HAVE SAME SIGN   ') 
8750     !  130 CONTINUE    
8751     !      AA = A      
8752     !      BB = B      
8753     !      MAXFNN = MAXFN
8754     !      RETURN      
8755     !      END 
8756
